人是誰都看不上眼的。

第四，社會上的矛盾現象使教師的信仰完全失却。兒童在教師那裏聽了一篇篇的大道理，再看看社會上客觀的環境，却有許多塲合與教師的話大相逕庭。兒童對於教師的信仰，起先不能不起動盪，終於有所懷疑了。比方說迷信無補於救國之道，這是兒童已常聞之於教　　四中，兒童也確信其有至理。但是落在他們眼前的事實，竟有人提倡念經　域，而且教師還督促他們去參加這種運動。對於教師言行的矛盾，他們的小心靈中自不能不起反感。至於教師怕摔破了飯碗，要迎合上司的心理，才教他們這麽幹的，這可他們不知道，就是知道，也不能相諒的。

綜合上述種種原因，要使教師地位不降落，實是萬不可能的！兒童是未來國家的柱石，使這個柱石穏固的責任是教師，教師旣負有重大的責任，自不應受人家鄙視，這已成爲了一種天經地義。至於教師自己方面的修養也是緊要的。教師是兒童理想的對象，教師的一舉一動，在在可以影響兒童的行爲。教師的言行應當一致，口裏說到那樣，就應做到那樣，這樣才可得到兒童的信仰，而使教授上感到方便，而且也只有這樣，教育事業纔能有展放曙光的希望。

請失業朋友注意

茲有某君在杭州從事著述，需用蒐集報紙雜誌材料繕寫文稿之助手一人，性别不拘，但以年在三十以内具有中學程度者爲較合適，能諳英日文字更佳，每日工作三小時，願就者請將學歷及希望報酬親筆函杭州學士路二十八號張宅。

某美術公司新發明婦女裝飾上之美術品，擴聘請推銷員數人，須熟悉衣飾店家或中大學校中之學生，能英文會話者尤佳，願應徵者請先投函新疆路德興里七號鄒君收轉。

本市白克路逸民里十三號大通新聞社擬添用實習記者二人，專門採訪本埠新聞，自問能勝任該項職務者，請撰新聞稿　篇，連同履歷，投寄該社。

茲徵求日文教假　位，須文法與會話兼重，每日授課一句鐘，時間聽便，住址不拘，月奉酬大洋十元，函商處徐家匯郵局轉交吳夢英。

敝處現有高小畢業程度學生一人，初小畢業程度學生二人，擬於暑期内聘請教師一位，補習英，國，算，三科，地點在法租界貝勒路

中段，如有此項人才而願受聘者，請開具履歷及最低限度之修金數目，函高昌廟海軍司令部葉耕甫代洽

社會醫藥　館欲招請本埠推銷員數位，如願就者不分性别，請先投函大沽路新馬安里三十四號該報館事務部收。

某小學擬聘請中年級及低年級級任女教師二名，須嫻於英文美術工藝歌舞體育各科，願就者請書明履歷及要求待遇投函本埠閘北物華路恊昌里四號周君轉。

某小學現欲添請國文教員一位，擔任高年級級任，並須熟悉公文，自問能勝任者可具函詳述履歷勝任學科及希望等投愛多亞路一三一○弄鋆樂邨三四號瞿崇儉醫師收。

茲需文經理數位，專事推銷，願任者請投函北站界路均益里十一號羣益公司接洽。

某校擴充學級，添聘男女教員數位，願就者請携帶證明文件赴楊樹浦路底三源坊三號與李秀珍女士面洽。

學世界語之良機

上海世界語者　會

設暑期世語講習班

上海世界語者恊會，向以傳授世界語爲己任，過去開設世界語講習班數屆，均成績斐然。茲以暑期將屆，特自七月九日起開暑期講習班二個月，以應學者之需。班次分初中二級，早晚班均有，學校僅收三元。簡章可向該會（上海卡德路永平坊十四號）索取。夫世界語優美易學久爲學者所推許，今能利用暑期學得此新時代的言語，實爲學者之良機。該會爲便利外埠學生計，且定有代覓宿所辦法云。

科學叢談

航空救國飛行船發明的故事（三）

— 叔麟

一七六六年，有名的英國化學者卡威台發見輕氣，發見輕氣是比空氣輕得多。在世界的氣球界，此實爲一大革命。

此後，愛登堡波拉克博士，開始作裝輕氣的氣球。博士在牛腸中放入輕氣，以重量過重而人敗。輕氣發見後，暫時無人利用牠。

經數年，法國蒙脫哥費兄弟作氣球的實騐，兄名司丹福，弟名喬許，他們原在阿諾奈區紙店裏的，偶然想到才製作氣球。有趣的是氣球及飛行機的發明，屢屢因兄弟的合作而成功。齊柏林和他弟弟哈勃脫的發明齊柏林飛行船，拉伊脫式飛行機的發明，都是兄弟倆合作成功的事實。蒙脫哥費兄弟以爲用許多紙作一只大大的袋子，裝入烟便可昇上天空了。

兄弟倆商量着，做了一隻大紙袋，這在紙店裏是極便當的。把那袋拿到庭中央，在其下面燃起乾草。

兄弟倆快活得出聲而笑，紙袋裏充滿了烟，便離開兄弟倆的手而上昇了。他倆仰起頭坐着，拍手鼓舞。自己的設計得到成功，歡喜自非無理的。但那個時候，袋並非因充滿烟而上昇，實因靠着空氣加熱變輕而被帶着上昇的。

接着蒙脫哥費兄弟再製作了第二個大氣球，膨脹成圓形，直徑有三十呎。

一七八三年六月五日這氣球預備在阿諾奈廣塲舉放。聞訊齊集者數千人。蒙脫哥費的氣球向着澄淸的空間靜靜上昇。觀者齊聲喝采，兄弟之得意可知。結果，在當時無疑的得到非常成功。氣球昇高一哩半，其中空氣漸漸冷却後便靜靜下降。

蒙脫哥費當時的氣球，當然還不能載貨乘人。

兄弟之成功，與人人以極大的刺激，製造氣球的人驟多。那年八月，有名的科學者愛姆，却而司與洛勃脫兄弟作一氣球，氣球的外皮用塗橡膠的薄綢做成，其中裝以輕氣。（未完）

1934.06.24

Northern Peiping Railway Bureau to Convene Final Through-Traffic Meeting Today, Discussing the Formation of the 'Peiping-Liaoning Travel Agency,' with Zhang Dezhi Scheduled as General Manager and Suzuki as Deputy General Manager; Two New Train Sets Prepared by the Northern Peiping Railway Factory to Undergo Track Testing; Unresolved Matters in the War Zone to Be Decided in Tianjin

(Peiping) The Northern Peiping Railway Bureau is scheduled to convene a final meeting in Tianjin tomorrow to discuss the formation of the Peiping-Liaoning Travel Agency, and has telegraphed invitations to representatives from the China Travel Service and the Japan Tourist Bureau to arrive in Tianjin on the 23rd. Zhou Sizhong, Vice President of the China Travel Service, Manager Chen Xiangtao, Assistant Manager Hu Shiyuan, and Committee Member Zhang Shuiqi, among others, arrived in Tianjin this morning. Suzuki, the representative from the Japan Tourist Bureau, is scheduled to arrive in Tianjin tonight from Dalian, accompanied by Major General Koyabu. Representatives from the Ministry of Railways will also participate. Tomorrow's discussion will be limited to matters concerning the establishment of the travel agency. It is reported that the authorities responsible for the preparations have decided to rename the Peiping-Liaoning Travel Agency as an agency, with its headquarters in Shanhaiguan and branch offices in Peiping and Tianjin. (23rd Dispatch)

(Peiping) Yin Tong stated that tomorrow's meeting will discuss matters related to the organization of the travel agency, and he will also participate. Through-traffic between Peiping and Shenyang can be realized by July 1st. However, with the shortening of the line, many railway staff have been laid off, making temporary borrowing this time particularly difficult. The organization of the travel agency has now been decided to use the name Peiping-Liaoning, to be prepared by the China Travel Service and the Japan Tourist Bureau, and is expected to be established by the end of this month. In terms of staffing, the railway bureau... Regarding negotiations in the war zone, he has met with Shibayama several times, and progress can be made after the through-traffic is implemented. When the Peiping-Shenyang through-train begins operation, it will only display a wooden sign for the Peiping-Liaoning Travel Agency. In the future, ticket sales locations will total six in Peiping: (1) Peiping-Liaoning Travel Agency Branch, (2) Northern Peiping Railway Qianmen Station, (3) China Travel Service, (4) Japan Tourist Bureau, (5) Thomas Cook & Son, (6) American Express. A commission of 5% will be earned for all ticket sales. (23rd Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Today at 11:30 AM, Yin Tong returned to Tianjin from Peiping. Yin's return to Tianjin is to prepare for the meeting convened in Tianjin on the 24th. The Japanese attendees at this meeting will include five representatives from the South Manchuria Railway, including Motomura, as well as Suzuki, the director of the Tianjin International Tourist Bureau and International Travel Agency. The Chinese representatives will include Chen Xiangtao and Zhou Shizhong, managers of the China Travel Service, as well as Hu Shiyuan, Qin Pingjiu, Zhang Shaochuan, and Zhang Xiaochuan. The Northern Peiping Railway will be represented by Yin Tong, Chen Qingwen, Director of the Transportation Department, Xu Ji, Director of the General Affairs Department, Wang Xuan, Director of the Accounting Department, and the chief inspector of the railway's transportation division. The meeting will be held at the Northern Peiping Railway's official residence or temporarily moved to the Northern Peiping Railway Bureau's reception area. This meeting will strictly discuss technical issues and will not discuss other matters. (23rd Dispatch)

(Tianjin) An important official of the Tianjin International Tourist Bureau stated that no one except those directly involved knows all the detailed procedures before the through-traffic. Currently, it is only known that the decision to implement it will be realized on July 1st. Regarding the agency handling the through-traffic, after inquiring from various parties today, it is said that it will be named the Oriental Travel Agency. (23rd Dispatch)

(Tianjin) It is rumored that Chen Xiangtao, manager of the China Travel Service, arrived in Tianjin this morning. However, the staff of the China Travel Service branch here welcomed him at the station at 7:30 AM but did not see him. Therefore, it is rumored that Chen arrived secretly on the Tianjin-Pukou train, and it is unknown where he is staying after disembarking. He has not been to the travel agency or met with anyone. However, important officials of the agency, Cai Pingjiu, Zhang Xiaochuan, Zhang Shaochuan, and Hu Shiyuan, came to Tianjin early at 7:30 AM and stayed at the Astor House Hotel. They refuse to confirm whether Chen has come to Tianjin and refuse to see visitors. (23rd Dispatch)

(Peiping) Yin Tong went to Tianjin this morning to continue negotiations on the Peiping-Shenyang through-traffic. Yin Rugeng and Shibayama are scheduled to attend tomorrow. (23rd Dispatch)

(Peiping) Chen Xiangtao, general manager of the China Travel Service, arrived in Tianjin today. The South Manchuria Railway also sent five Japanese technicians to Peiping. A preparatory meeting was convened once this morning to plan all the procedures. The Tianjin meeting is reportedly scheduled for the 25th. (23rd Dispatch)

(Peiping) Two new train sets manufactured by the Tangshan Railway Factory of the Northern Peiping Railway were released from the factory today and are undergoing test runs between Tangshan and Luanxian. The train is entirely gray in color, with an aesthetically pleasing interior layout. It is scheduled to depart for Fengtai on the 29th. The train includes one first-class dining car, one sleeping car, two second-class cars, four third-class cars, and one baggage/guard car and one postal car. The Japan Tourist Bureau stated that the East Asia headquarters of the Japan Tourist Bureau is located in Dalian, with Saito as the general manager. A tourist bureau is also set up within the Ministry of Railways, and Suzuki is a director of that bureau. Suzuki previously went to Dalian or is going to Tianjin to represent and attend the meeting. The tourist bureau has a branch in Shanhaiguan, with Kamihara as the manager, Kitajo as the manager of the Peiping branch, Kiyomoto as the manager of the Tianjin branch, and Yoshida as the manager of the Shenyang branch. Currently, the Peiping and other local branches are selling through-transportation tickets. (23rd Dispatch)

(Peiping) During a meeting with Japanese personnel in Dalian, Yin Tong requested that after the train operations begin, everything must be handled in accordance with Chinese law. Initially, the Japanese side strongly argued against this, but after both sides made every effort to negotiate, the Japanese side finally agreed to concede. (23rd Dispatch)

(Tianjin) This afternoon, after returning to Tianjin, Yin Tong immediately convened a meeting of important department heads and section chiefs at the Railway Bureau to secretly instruct them on all preparations before the through-traffic. Chen Xiangtao met with Yin Tong at the Northern Peiping Park at 3:00 PM this afternoon for an informal discussion. Participants from the Northern Peiping Railway included Xu Ji, Director of the General Affairs Department, Chen Qingwen, Director of the Mechanical Department, Wang Xuan, Director of the Accounting Department, and Bao Leifan, Director of the Transportation Division. Participants from the China Travel Service included Zhou Shizhong, Hu Shiyuan, Zhang Shaochuan, Cai Pingsheng, and Zhang Xiaochuan. The consultation lasted for two hours before adjourning. (23rd Dispatch)

(Peiping) The unresolved issues in the war zone are gradually developing as the through-traffic is about to be realized. Yin Rugeng and Tao Shangming are scheduled to go to Tianjin tomorrow to earnestly discuss and resolve matters with Shibayama and others. It is reported that there are about five issues on the agenda: (1) The number of New Peacekeeping Force troops to be dispatched will be standardized at 6,000 men. A certain amount of light weapons may be carried at discretion. The dispatch period can be determined after negotiations are settled in Tianjin. (2) To crack down on Japanese and Korean ruffians selling drugs in the war zone, it is proposed to request that the Japanese side order local garrison commanders not to protect them any further and to assist in the investigation and prohibition. (3) To take over Malanyu and safeguard the Eastern Tombs, except for the administrative part of Malanyu, which has already been taken over, it is hoped that the Japanese puppet troops will withdraw outside the pass within a short period of time. (4) The puppet police in Nantianmen should quickly withdraw from Gubeikou to outside the Great Wall line as agreed. (5) The Japanese puppet troops in Xifengkou, Saheqiao, and Lengkou Jianchangying should be moved outside the Great Wall line. It is intended that the above issues should be completely resolved as soon as possible in accordance with the previous agreement in the Yuguan meeting. As for abolishing the Tanggu Truce, the Japanese side has not yet made any statement. It is reported that it will be reviewed after Huang returns north. According to the Japanese side, if the Peiping-Shenyang through-traffic is realized, all problems will be easily resolved. (23rd Dispatch)

Gubeikou Puppet Police Completely Withdraw North

(Peiping) A Gubeikou dispatch states that the puppet police of the Puppet National Border Police Headquarters, numbering more than 50, led by the Captain Hong Lu, completely withdrew from outside the South Gate to the Juhe Inn at Erdaoqiao outside the North Gate yesterday morning. They will move in after the houses are built. The more than 10 puppet police who withdrew from Nantianmen are still stationed at the old site of the Puppet First National Road Bureau inside the North Gate. The puppet police at the Caojialukou withdrew to the Xiaobaichi Township outside Baimaguan. Liu Wandi, director of the Miyun Public Security Bureau, sent Ruan Wenying with 10 police officers to Caojialu yesterday to take over the defense. (23rd Dispatch)

Guerrillas Attack Freight Train Near Yimianpo

(Harbin) At 5:15 PM today, a freight train of the Chinese Eastern Railway was attacked by guerrillas while heading west, about 28 miles east of Yimianpo. The train was destroyed, the driver was killed, and five people were injured. The guerrillas first removed the fishplates from the rails. When the train passed the area, the locomotive and four freight cars derailed and overturned. The guerrillas ambushed on both sides and opened fire. They then robbed the goods from the train and took away the uninjured crew members. (Reuters, 23rd)

Korean Immigrants Clash with Chinese Farmers in Banqiaozi

(Shenyang) According to a local newspaper report, 100 Korean immigrants clashed with 500 Chinese farmers in Laoshilu within the jurisdiction of Banqiaozi early on the 20th. After a major brawl, four Koreans were injured, and one is missing. A large team of Japanese police went to suppress the clash and arrested 10 Chinese people. The cause of the conflict appears to be a dispute over water. The situation is still at a stalemate. (Hualian, 23rd)

Miao Shiliang, Correspondent for the Harbin International Cooperation News, Arrested by Japanese Military Police

(Tianjin) Miao Shiliang, a correspondent for the Harbin International Cooperation News, recently returned to his hometown to visit relatives. He was arrested by the Japanese military police on the 23rd upon his return to Harbin, accused of leaking anti-Manchu news to China. He is currently still in custody and is not allowed bail. (23rd Dispatch)

Yamamoto, Japanese National Kidnapped from the Shuntian Steamer, Returned to Tianjin Yesterday; Naval Aircraft to Depart Today for Reconnaissance of Bandits

(Tianjin) Yamamoto, the Japanese national kidnapped in the Shuntian Steamer case, returned to Tianjin from Tanggu by car early this morning. In the afternoon, he went to the Japanese Consulate to meet with Consul-General Chahara to describe his experiences. Rumors that Yamamoto brought back bandit demands are not confirmed. (23rd Dispatch)

(Qingdao) Naval aircraft, due to rain on the 23rd, changed to fly to the Yellow River Estuary on the 24th to cooperate in suppressing sea bandits. (23rd)

(Yantai) The condition of third mate Ross of the Shuntian Steamer is optimistic today, with hopes for a complete recovery. His temperature and pulse are normal, and his appetite is good. His mother is very relieved and visits him during the times allowed by the doctor. (Reuters, 23rd)

British Ambassador Arrives in Weihaiwei

(Weihaiwei) British Ambassador Sir Miles Lampson and his wife, accompanied by their three children, arrived here today aboard the British warship HMS Folkestone. They will stay for a week. Admiral Sir Frederick Dreyer, Commander-in-Chief of the British China Station, is hosting a banquet aboard the British warship HMS Suffolk tonight to entertain them. A dance will be held after the banquet, and a regatta for the crew members is scheduled for Monday. (Reuters, 23rd)

Supervisory Yuan's Administrative Meeting Decides to First Establish Supervisory Commissioner's Offices in Jiangsu and Hebei

(Nanjing) The Supervisory Yuan held its 29th Administrative Meeting on the 23rd, attended by more than 50 supervisory committee members, including Liu Eqing. Yu Youren presided over the meeting. Many important cases were discussed, and it was decided to first establish Supervisory Commissioner's Offices in Jiangsu and Hebei provinces. The remaining districts will be established successively. The candidates for Supervisory Commissioner have not yet been determined. (Central News Agency, 23rd)

(Nanjing) The Supervisory Yuan held an expanded administrative meeting on the 23rd, with Yu Youren presiding. 1. It was decided to establish Supervisory Commissioner's Offices by district. In addition to the original 12 districts, the following districts were added: 1. Anhui-Jiangxi, 2. Jiangsu, 3. Henan-Shandong, 4. Hubei. 2. It was decided to increase the scope of investigation effectiveness. In the past, when the Supervisory Yuan sent supervisory committee members to various provinces for investigation, the only assistance they received was from the police authorities, and the scope of effectiveness was too small. It is proposed to expand the scope to include all provincial and county party headquarters and administrative organs within the scope of assistance. (23rd Dispatch)

Chairman Chiang Kai-shek Gives Instructions at the Central Political School; To Leave for Hangzhou from Nanking Tomorrow

(Nanjing) Chairman Chiang Kai-shek went to the Central Political School at 10:00 AM on the 23rd to give instructions, mainly stating that the academic atmosphere and discipline of the Central Political School are praised by Chinese and foreigners, and students should pay attention to: (1) physical health, (2) starting from self-cultivation and family harmony to achieve the goal of governing the country and bringing peace to the world. After Chiang finished his instructions, he went to the principal's office to discuss school affairs with school committee members Chen Guofu, Luo Jialun, and Wu Yifeng, and instructed on the important facilities and directions for this year. He returned to his residence at noon. (Central News Agency, 23rd)

(Nanjing) A senior staff officer of the Military Council stated that Chairman Chiang is scheduled to depart on the 25th, taking the through-train between Nanjing, Shanghai, and Hangzhou straight to Hangzhou. He intends to not stop in Shanghai, will stay in Hangzhou for several days, and then return to Jiangxi to preside over the suppression of bandits. (23rd Dispatch)

(Nanjing) The Central Political School held the graduation ceremony for its third graduating class on the morning of the 23rd. Chiang personally attended and gave instructions. Chiang was originally scheduled to inspect the Political Research Institute of the Military Council on the 23rd, but because he attended the graduation ceremony of the Central Political School, he was unable to go. He temporarily notified the school to postpone the inspection to 9:00 AM on the 24th. (23rd Dispatch)

(Hangzhou) Provincial Secretary-General Lu Dai telegraphed the Provincial Government on the evening of the 23rd, stating that Chairman Chiang is scheduled to come to Hangzhou on the 25th. Lu himself left Nanjing that evening. The Provincial Government has telegraphed Lu Dipeng to report. (23rd)

Chiang Plans to Implement a Policy of Military Reclamation and Border Colonization; Trial Implementation of a Military-Industrial Construction Plan

(Nanjing) It is reported that after the military suppression of bandits ends, Chairman Chiang plans to distribute troops to key areas in the border regions to implement a policy of military reclamation and border colonization, and to trial implement a military-industrial construction plan, with the aim of using organized forces to revive the countryside and promote production. (23rd Dispatch)

Southwestern Political Council Holds Discussion Meeting Yesterday; Exchanges Views on National Defense and Bandit Suppression; Prepares to Submit to a Joint Meeting

(Hong Kong) The Southwestern Political Council held a discussion meeting on the 23rd, attended by Xiao Focheng, Deng Zhiru, Zou Lu, Chen Jitang, Li Zongren, Bai Chongxi, and Tang Shaoyi. They exchanged views on national defense and bandit suppression and are preparing to submit them to a joint meeting of the Executive Department and Political Council on the 24th. He Jian was also invited to attend. He Jian met with the press at Tuisi Garden on the morning of the 23rd and issued a written statement, stating that he came to Guangdong voluntarily to discuss with Chen, Li, and Bai the joint suppression of communists and the pacification of bandits on the border between Hunan and Guangdong. He Jian went to Nanchang last month and stayed for a week. He will stay in Guangdong for three or four days and then return to Hunan. (33rd Dispatch)

(Hong Kong) Hunanese living in Guangdong held a meeting at noon on the 23rd to welcome He Jian. The heads of the various Guangdong departments hosted a banquet for He in the evening. Xiao Focheng said on the 23rd that He Jian and Guangdong have basically agreed on bandit suppression, and a decision will be made after further discussion with Chen Jitang, Li and Bai. (23rd Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Hunan Chairman He Jian was ordered to go to Guangdong to participate in the meeting of the three southwestern provinces. He recently telegraphed Nanking to report on the progress of the negotiations. It is said that He's negotiations in Guangdong are proceeding smoothly. (23rd Dispatch)

Kong Xiangxi Passed Through Jinan Yesterday; Han Fuju and Others Greeted Him at the Station

(Jinan) Today, Kong Xiangxi passed through Yanzhou and Taian, where he was greeted with grand welcomes. When he passed through Jinan, Han Fuju and important figures from various circles, as well as fellow villagers from Shanxi and Shaanxi residing in Shandong, greeted him at the station. Kong got off the train and talked with Han in the parlor for half an hour, discussing ways to deal with the aftermath of salt smuggling along the coast of the province. Han urged Kong to get off the train, but Kong said that he had to rush to Peiping on the 25th and would return north on the original train at 5:00 PM. In the train, he told Yu Gu that Shandong's politics were excellent, but local products were declining tragically. Although the central government has repeatedly reduced taxes, exports last year were still 6.5% lower than the previous year. This is because the goods have not been improved, and it is hoped that the authorities will assist the business community in seeking improvement as soon as possible. Furthermore, there is a lot of smuggling along the coast, causing great losses to customs. Setting up checkpoints and investigating smuggling has already collected taxes, as has the Changcheng Pass. This is not about setting up customs to collect taxes. There have been three robberies of 10,000 dan of salt in Weihaiwei. Fortunately, the provincial government and the navy have made every effort to maintain peace and have been pacified. The government should be considerate of the people, but those who disregard the law should also be dealt with according to the law. In addition to inspecting Hebei, Henan, Shandong, and Shanxi, if there is time on this trip, he plans to go to Suiyuan and Shaanxi and then come to Xuzhou in the north for inspection. It will take about four weeks to return to Nanjing after Jinan and Qingdao. (23rd Dispatch)

(Xuzhou) Kong Xiangxi passed through Xuzhou at 6:00 AM on the 23rd, attaching to the Tianjin-Pukou chartered train to the north. (23rd Dispatch)

(Peiping) Kong Xiangxi left Nanking last night to inspect the financial situation in North China and to attend the graduation ceremony of Yenching University. Ning Encheng, director of the Hebei, Shanxi, Chahar, and Suiyuan Consolidated Tax Bureau, Ding Chungao, director of the Hebei Stamp Tax Bureau, Yu Jinhe, director of the Peiping Public Security Bureau, and others are going to Tianjin tonight to meet him. Kong will stay in Peiping for about two weeks, and then go to Shanxi to visit Yan's illness and measure the Fen River. After completing his official duties in Taiyuan, he will return to his ancestral home in Taigu to visit relatives. (23rd Dispatch)

Weihaiwei Villagers Rob Salt Incident; Audit Office Asks Xu Dongfan to Investigate

(Jinan) 30,000 dan of salt was robbed by villagers in Weihaiwei. The Audit Office has asked Xu Dongfan to investigate the ringleaders and pursue the salt tax. There are rumors in Yexian and Changyi Xiaying that villagers will rise up again to rob salt. An investigation has revealed that there is no movement. Han Fuju advised the Audit Office to send people to various coastal areas to explain. (23rd Dispatch)

(Jinan) Han Fuju said that although salt miners rob salt is illegal, we should also seek a radical solution. (23rd Dispatch)

Lu Fengnian's Troops Ordered to Be Transferred to Jiangxi for Training; Lu Arrived in Peiping the Night Before to Meet with He; Returns to His Garrison Today; Departure Date and Procedures Have Been Decided

(Peiping) Lu Fengnian's troops have been ordered to be transferred to Nanchang for training. Lu himself came to Peiping on the night of the 22nd to meet with Chairman He, requesting instructions on the departure date and procedures. It was decided: (1) to start moving out of Wangdu on the 25th; (2) to receive firearms after arriving in Jiangxi; (3) to allocate defense zones after arrival; (4) to continue to distribute supplies from the Peiping branch; (5) to issue 20 days' worth of supplies to eliminated officers and soldiers and to dismiss them by the 24th; (6) to send the sick to the Garrison Hospital for treatment. Lu is scheduled to return to his garrison on the morning of the 24th to handle everything. On the 23rd, he also sent Guo Tiefu, a staff officer of the Department, and others to Jiujiang and Hankou to prepare the forward stations. (Central News Agency, 23rd)

Amoy Situation Eases; Arrested Japanese Residents Handed Over to the Japanese Consulate

(Amoy) A bomb exploded in front of the Southeast Hotel opened by Japanese residents on the night of the 22nd. According to injured rickshaw puller Shi Shuihui, who witnessed it, four people came out of [illegible], threw the bomb on the road, re-entered [illegible], and went upstairs. The bomb was thrown by someone from a certain side, intending to create a serious situation. That night, on the pretext of this, hundreds of people carrying guns demonstrated everywhere. The situation has eased on the 23rd. The Public Security Bureau arrested five Japanese gamblers on the 20th and handed them over to the Japanese Consulate on the 22nd. (23rd Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Yan Huiqing passed through Nanking from Shanghai on the evening of the 23rd to the north. (23rd Dispatch)

Current Commentary

The Triangular Conflict of Naval Arms Reduction

— Jing

The preliminary talks for the naval arms reduction conference attended by Great Britain, the United States, and Japan have begun in London. What will be the final outcome? By carefully observing the unofficial opinions expressed by these three countries, we can get a glimpse of the general situation. Let us first discuss Great Britain. In principle, it wants to do its best to maintain the status quo of the world. However, it absolutely does not want the excessive growth of French power on the European continent. The struggle between France and Italy for dominance in the Mediterranean is becoming increasingly blatant. Although Great Britain has not taken sides, its psychology of using the conflict between France and Italy to maintain its special navigation rights in the Strait of Gibraltar and the Suez Canal cannot be concealed. As for the relationship between Great Britain and Germany, it is clearly different from before the war. Although Germany today is not without long-term plans, its strength is limited. Opposing the Soviet Union is just empty talk. Its original intention is to figure out how to get rid of the shackles of the Treaty of Versailles. The desires of the Germans have long been understood by Great Britain, so it does not hesitate to show favor to Germany in order to suppress France. In the Far East, Great Britain does not want the expansion of American economic power, and even more does not want the Soviet Union to come out to the east. Therefore, it provides Japan with convenience everywhere. It does not know that this strategy has actually helped Japan achieve a situation of dominating East Asia, and even threatens India. Great Britain cannot unite with the United States to contain Japan, nor is it willing to be in a position of failure, so it plans to add cruisers and other auxiliary vessels to consolidate its vested interests in the Far East.

Japan believes that the discussion of naval technical issues, such as the reduction of battleships, the limitation of heavy cruisers, and the abolition of aircraft carriers, are all errors of the Washington and London conferences. From Japan's perspective, raising these kinds of issues will cause Great Britain and the United States to coordinate and fall into a state of isolation. Therefore, it changed its strategy and proposed its vaunted principle of military equality, and clearly stated that Japan has no intention of invading the West at this moment. As for the market issues of India and British directly administered colonies, it is also willing to gradually consult with Great Britain to ease the hostility of the trade war between the two countries. Japan's goal is nothing more than to slowly implement its continental policy, destroying British and American cooperation on the one hand, and facilitating its dominance in the Western Pacific on the other.

The United States' attempt to open up markets is not as aggressive as it used to be. The Washington authorities are deeply afraid of causing disputes again due to naval issues. Therefore, it proposes to extend the London Naval Treaty to prove that it has no aggressive intentions towards foreign countries. Even if European countries do not repay war debts, the United States has not yet made any positive statements except to propose passive countermeasures. This is enough to show that the American mentality is determined to eliminate the domestic economic panic as the top priority. Because of the existence of this psychology, it only declares the maintenance of the open-door policy toward China. It is even abandoning special interests in the Philippines and allowing it to become independent. However, whether the independence of the Philippines can match its name in reality and not be threatened by Japanese hegemony is still questionable. The Philippines has a lot of room for development and is only separated from Tainan by a narrow strip of water. The Japanese will inevitably bring their political immigration policy and economic dumping policy with them. Filipinos will have no way to protect themselves. Although there are rumors that the United States has asked Great Britain to jointly guarantee the neutrality of the Philippines, it is difficult to expect success due to Great Britain's own contradictions. It is expected that the result of the 1935 naval arms reduction conference will only make the conflict between the three countries more and more acute.

Zhang Ji Returned to Xi'an Yesterday

(Xi'an) Zhang Ji went to the Zhongnan Mountains south of the city on the 9th to inspect the highway built by the Western Capital Planning Committee. He did not return to the city until last night. He stayed in the countryside for more than ten days. According to him, the highway south of the city has been completed. The scenery in Zhongnan Mountain, Cuihua Mountain, and Tangyu is excellent, making people forget to return. Cuihua Mountain has Jiangtang, ice caves, and waterfalls. The ice caves are frozen all year round. Tangyu has natural hot springs. They were all the most prosperous areas in the Tang Dynasty and have been abandoned. It is now planned to repair them and make them the best scenery in the Western Capital in the future. (Central News Agency, 23rd)

Mongolian Political Council Submits a Request to Amend the Organizational Regulations

(Nanjing) The Mongolian Political Council telegraphed the central government requesting that the temporary organizational regulations of the Mongolian Political Council be amended. (23rd Dispatch)

Three Measures Decided for Dredging Poyang Lake

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Interior convened representatives from the Ministry of Communications and Jiangxi Province on the 23rd to discuss ways to dredge Poyang Lake. It was decided: (1) The entire lake's topography will be surveyed. The Ministry of Interior and the Ministry of Communications will ask the Naval Aviation Survey Team to carry out the survey on their behalf. (2) Waterway surveys will be the responsibility of the Yangtze River Water Conservancy Commission of the Ministry of Communications. (3) The dredging project from Hukou to the Yangtze River should be carried out as soon as possible. The Jiangxi Provincial Government will jointly formulate a plan with the Yangtze River Water Conservancy Commission, solicit labor and implement it. The Jiangxi Provincial Government will submit a request to the Nanchang Headquarters for appropriate assistance with the required funding, and the Ministry of Interior and the Ministry of Communications will jointly submit a report to the Executive Yuan, and issue a letter to the Economic Committee to transfer the Jiangxi Office to find a way to subsidize. The result of the consultation will be reported to the Executive Yuan by the Ministry of Interior and the Ministry of Communications. (23rd Dispatch)

Lu Dipeng, Due to Illness, Chiang Orders Continued Leave for Recuperation

(Nanjing) Lu Dipeng's spirit has not recovered, and he sent Lu Dai to Nanking to meet with Chiang. Chiang instructed Lu Dai to inform Chairman Lu to continue his leave for recuperation so that he can recover his health as soon as possible. As for the political situation in Zhejiang Province, he will convene a meeting of the directors of various institutes after arriving in Hangzhou to discuss and resolve it. Lu Dai returned to Hangzhou on the 23rd after receiving instructions. (23rd Dispatch)

The Flood in Gan River Gradually Recedes

(Nanchang) Since the Gan River has surged, the disasters in the counties along the coast are worrying. According to the Water Conservancy Bureau on the 23rd, reports came from Fengcheng and Ji'an that the flood is gradually receding, and the water level in Nanchang has also dropped by four feet, which is a great comfort to the people. (Central News Agency, 23rd)

(Nanchang) The water level of the Gan River reached 35 feet on the 23rd. The weather is still cloudy and cold, and there is a continuous surge. Low-lying areas along the river in this city are flooded. On the opposite bank, the continent is a vast expanse of water. Most of the residents on the continent have entered the city to take refuge. The fields and crops on the lower continents are mostly submerged. The embankments are being strengthened for protection. The Gan-Xiang Road was suspended due to flooding. Pingxiang has run out of salt and light food. A telegram was sent to change the route to transport salt from Hunan and Hubei to provide emergency relief. More than ten feet of the embankment on the beach collapsed. The fields and crops inside Tingfeng embankment were completely flooded. (23rd Dispatch)

Heavy Rain in Hunan Province Causes Disaster

(Changsha) Continuous heavy rain, the water is thirty-three feet high, the provincial river floods into the city, and the counties have reported disasters, inland and water traffic in the province has stopped. (23rd Dispatch)

Hubei Provincial Government Borrows Money to Distribute Political Expenses

(Hankou) The provincial government borrowed 300,000 yuan from 15 banks, including the Bank of China, to distribute political expenses, and overdrawn 200,000 yuan from the Provincial Bank to repair the government building. It used public bonds as collateral and designated business tax for repayment. (23rd Dispatch)

Gang 行 Camp Sends Personnel to Investigate Bandit Areas, Implementing Soil Locking Work

(Nanchang) The Gang Eight One County's Sixth Special Political Bureau has already implemented blockades in six or seven county bureaus. In order to intensify the blockade and prevent abuses, the Camp has dispatched Jiang Xiaoan and twenty other personnel to various places for investigation and supervision. (23rd Special Dispatch)

Sichuan Bandit Suppression Army Captures Tongjiang County Seat

(Chongqing) The troops under Xu Shaozong, the division commander of the Fifth Route Army of the Sichuan Bandit Suppression, occupied Zhenlongguan on the 21st. Qin Shaozeng, the deputy commander-in-chief, captured Tongjiang County on the 22nd. The remaining bandits were routed. Xu's bandits moved forward, but due to the heavy troops defending in Gansu, Shaanxi, and Hubei, the main force shifted to the right. (23rd Special Dispatch)

(Hankou) Tang Shizun and Fan Shaozeng telegraphed Han, stating that Zhou Shaoxuan's brigade captured Tongjiang on the evening of the 21st. Four or five thousand remnants of the bandits retreated towards Hongkou and Maoyankou. Zhenlongguan, Mashichang, and Tumenchang were also recovered simultaneously. The bandits on the front of Wanyuan were also under significant threat. (23rd Special Dispatch)

Fujian Western Garrison Transfers Officers to Gang to Join the Lushan Officer Training Corps

(Xiamen) For the first session of the Lushan Officer Training Corps, more than fifty people including Li Zhaoliang and Yu Jinyuan from the deputy division commanders, brigade commanders, regimental commanders, and staff officers of the 39th, 83rd, and 36th divisions, were transferred from western Fujian to Gang for training. They arrived in Xiamen on the 22nd and took the Jinan transport ship to Shanghai for transfer. After graduating in March, they will return to their original positions. Song Xilian, the division commander of the 36th division, will serve as a company commander in the training corps and has already departed. (23rd Special Dispatch)

Taining's Order Completely Restored, Bandits from Tongan Flee to Zhangtai

(Fuzhou) Tang Enbo telegraphed the province, stating that after the recovery of Taining, order has been completely restored. The Fourth Division is currently working with the Gang army to build the Taining to Nanfeng highway, which is expected to be completed by the end of the month. (22nd Central News Agency Electric Dispatch)

(Fuzhou) Tongan County reported that the bandits who disturbed Guankou, claiming to be the South China State, led by the bandit leader Chen Hu, etc., were routed by the 87th Division troops and fled towards Zhangtai. (22nd Central News Agency Electric Dispatch)

(Fuzhou) Military Intelligence: The Tenth Column is advancing into Changting and has established firm contact with the Fourth Column. More than 20,000 bandits in Ting are now scattered in Ninghua, attempting to relieve the siege of Ting. However, our army is still actively developing, and the vanguard Sun Division has reached the edge of Ting. The bandits in both Ting and Ning are not difficult to completely resolve. (23rd Special Dispatch)

(Xiamen) Military intelligence indicates that the bandits of the 135th Army Corps are entrenched in the northeast and northwest of Liancheng. They engaged in fierce battles with our 9th Division on the 16th and 17th. The bandits suffered heavy casualties. According to reports, Zhu De is hastily building defensive works in Changting. Our side will launch a general offensive towards Changting as soon as the main force is fully deployed in Liancheng. At the same time, the southern route will advance from Yunmenling towards Huichang. (23rd Special Dispatch)

Zhengjiafang Confirmed Recaptured

(Hangzhou) It is confirmed that Zhengjiafang has been occupied by the Zhejiang Security Force. The battle was extremely fierce. Yu Jishi, the director of the Zhejiang Security Department, personally led his team to the front lines on the evening of the 17th to command. The next morning, they encircled the bandits from all sides, and after a fierce battle, they recaptured the area. Zhengjiafang is located between Yushan and Shangrao, with fertile land and abundant resources. The bandits intended to occupy it for a long time and had built extremely solid defensive structures such as bunkers, wooden fences, barbed wire, landmines, and outer moats in Tiger Rock and other places west of Zhengjiafang. Thanks to the bravery of the soldiers, it was recaptured this time. The people of Yushan are scheduled to hold a celebration meeting on the 24th. (23rd Central News Agency Electric Dispatch)

Ye Muhua Case: Personnel Sent to Japan to Investigate the Truth

(Nanjing) In addition to Minister Jiang negotiating with Japan regarding the Ye Muhua murder case, various circles in the capital are forming a Ye Case Support Association. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission have decided to send personnel to Japan to investigate the truth and use it as a basis for negotiation. Once the personnel are determined, they will depart immediately. (23rd Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Various overseas Chinese organizations in the capital held a meeting at the Overseas Chinese Reception Center at 3:00 PM on the 23rd. More than sixty people attended and discussed the case of Ye Muhua's brutal murder by the Japanese. Resolutions: (1) Request the Central Government and the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission to transfer the case to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for serious negotiation; (2) Send a telegram to various organizations at home and abroad for unified assistance; (3) Appoint representatives to petition the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and draft a telegram. (23rd Central News Agency Electric Dispatch)

Ministry of Communications Rectifies the Accounting System

(Nanjing) Zhu Jiahua, the Minister of Communications, believes that developing telecommunications requires first rectifying the accounting system. Last year, the accounting departments of various telegraph bureaus were completely separated, and accounting directors were established, directly under the Accounting Director's Office of the Ministry. Recently, following the independent accounting system of the Directorate-General of Budget, Accounting and Statistics, it was stipulated that the appointment and dismissal of accounting personnel in the future will be managed by the Directorate-General of Budget, Accounting and Statistics, without being subject to the control or interference of主管 personnel, and a committee for revising the telecommunications accounting system was organized to revise the accounting system. A circular has been issued to all telegraph bureaus and stations across the country, requiring them to strictly follow and implement the new system starting from the 23rd fiscal year. (23rd Central News Agency Electric Dispatch)

Ma Heng Discusses Methods for Improving the National Palace Museum

(Nanjing) Ma Heng discussed that the methods for improving the National Palace Museum proposed by him have been decided by Cai Yuanpei. The second board meeting will be held in Beijing on July 5th to discuss the methods of improvement and reorganization, as well as the storage plan, as follows: A. Methods to be organized at present: (1) Accelerate inventory; (2) Detailed classification; (3) Registration and boxing; (4) Reorganization of palaces for storing items other than warehouses; (5) Fundamental solutions for the relocation of cultural relics to the south; (6) Expedite the construction of the Nanjing warehouse; (7) Disposal of cultural relics unrelated to culture. B. Future storage methods: (1) Centralization of cultural relics stored in Shanghai; (2) Scientific organization of the storage system; (3) Formulation of various storage regulations; (4) Compilation and printing of catalogs after the organization of cultural relics. (23rd Central News Agency Electric Dispatch)

German Envoy Goes to Beidaihe for Summer Resort

(Beiping) German envoy Trautmann went to Tianjin this morning and then to Beidaihe for a summer resort. (23rd Special Dispatch)

Hebei Department of Finance Plans to Compile a Report on the Abolition of Exorbitant Taxes

(Tianjin) The Hebei Department of Finance has compiled a report on the methods for abolishing exorbitant taxes and various compensation issues, and submitted it to the provincial government for review. It is planned to be studied with Finance Minister Kong. (23rd Central News Agency Electric Dispatch)

Shandong Provincial School Military Instructor Conference

(Jinan) The Summer Military Training Committee convened a meeting of military instructors from various schools today to discuss the date of student gathering at each school and the training regulations. (23rd Special Dispatch)

Shaanxi Armory Constructed the Xi'an-Lanzhou Road, Inauguration Ceremony Held Yesterday

(Xi'an) The Shaanxi Armory built the Xi'an-Lanzhou Highway. The inauguration ceremony was held at Xiguan at 9:00 AM on the 23rd. About 5,000 people from all walks of life and the armory attended. Yang Hucheng and Chief of Staff Han Weixi reported on the commercial righteousness of the armory building the road. Shao Lizi, Zhang Ji, Liu Rusong, and others all gave speeches, expressing their satisfaction with the efforts of the Northwest Army in building the road. After the ceremony, construction started immediately from Xiguan, and the Longdong armory also started construction at the same time. (23rd Central News Agency Electric Dispatch)

Liu Zhenhua Went to Huangchuan to Meet Zhang

(Hankou) Liu Zhenhua went from Liu'an to Huangchuan to go to the front to meet Zhang Xueliang, discussing military affairs for the bandit suppression in the border areas, and welcoming Zhang to inspect the Anhui border. (23rd Special Dispatch)

Zhu Jingnong Telegraphed Resignation as Director of Hunan Education Department

(Changsha) Zhu Jingnong, Director of the Education Department, telegraphed Beijing to resign. The provincial government telegraphed the central government to persuade him to stay. (23rd Special Dispatch)

Camp Sends Personnel to Inspect Hunan-Hubei Local Corps

(Changsha) The Nanchang Camp specially dispatched Guo Yiyu, He Zhihao, and Zhou Nan as inspection commissioners for the Hunan-Hubei region, with Guo as the director. They arrived in Hunan on the morning of the 21st and inspected the Changsha Volunteer Corps and the Hunan University Military Training Class on the 23rd. After the inspection of the provincial capital is completed, they will go to various regions to inspect the security corps. (23rd Central News Agency Electric Dispatch)

Hunan Provincial Local Corps to Be Reformed into a Conscription System

(Changsha) The Hunan Provincial Local Corps will be reformed into a conscription system, with He Jian concurrently serving as the Director-General of Conscription and Training Corps Commander. (23rd Special Dispatch)

Japanese Military Officer Kobayashi Arrives at Majiang

(Fuzhou) Japanese Attache Kobayashi, accompanied by the commander of the Mashan Naval Port, arrived at Majiang on the Kumano cruiser on the morning of the 23rd. He went to the Hayakaze destroyer stationed in Ma and conveyed the Japanese Emperor's decree to all officers and soldiers below the captain. Then, he and the Kumano Captain Horiuchi, etc., arrived in the province, unofficially visiting Chinese and Japanese officials and inspecting the situation of Japanese residents. (23rd Special Dispatch)

Continuous Rain in Fuzhou, the Minjiang River Rises

(Fuzhou) There has been continuous rain in the city for half a month, the upstream water has risen, and stream floods have recurred. Low-lying areas have become swamps, and transportation on the city platform has gradually been cut off, causing considerable losses to farmland. The water level receded slightly on the evening of the 21st. The highway project has been severely damaged. According to investigations, the Quanlong Road was washed away by the water, and the roadbed collapsed. The Construction Department sent engineer Chen Qihua to rush to repair it. The Shaoguang Road was also affected by the water. The Pucheng section was originally scheduled to open to traffic on the 20th, and the Xiafu section was originally scheduled to open to traffic on the 16th, but both have been postponed due to flood obstruction. (22nd Central News Agency Electric Dispatch)

Guangdong Dredging Bureau Handles the Construction Work of Huangpu Port

(Guangzhou) The Guangdong Provincial Dredging Bureau is actively handling the construction work of Huangpu Port. It has been decided today to divide the area into twelve zones, including: (1) Industrial zone, with warehouses, wharves, shipyards, and coal yards all located here; (2) Administrative zone; (3) Industrial zone; (4) Handicraft zone; (5) Wholesale zone for goods; (6) Retail zone for goods; (7) First-class residential zone; (8) Second-class residential zone; (9) Third-class residential zone; (10) Agricultural zone; (11) Entertainment zone; (12) Cemetery zone. (23rd Reuters Electric Dispatch)

Huang Shaoxiong Went from Rong County to Yong

(Hong Kong) Huang Shaoxiong met with Bai Chongxi in Wu. He is now going from Rong County to Yong to meet Huang Xuchu, staying for a few days before returning to Rong County. (23rd Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Huang Shaoxiong telegraphed Beijing, stating that he met with Hu Hanmin in Hong Kong and exchanged opinions on the current situation. Hu expressed that it was quite good. Hu approved the central government and the southwest to cooperate, first striving to suppress the communist bandits, and then negotiating on party affairs and government affairs to seek improvement in national affairs. (23rd Special Dispatch)

International Commercial Telegraph

June 23rd, Reuters Exclusive Commercial News Telegraph

Gold and Silver

▲London Gold Price: The London gold price today is 138 shillings and 1 pence, the same as yesterday's price.

▲London Silver Bar: The London silver market today, spot is 20 pence and 3125, forward is 20 pence and 375, both up 25 from yesterday's close. Today, Indian firms and speculators bought, while China sold. The close was stable.

▲Bombay Silver Bar: The Bombay silver market soared today and closed stable. Spot rose 13 annas to 56 rupees and 8 annas. Futures also rose 12 annas.

Exchange Rate

▲US-UK: The New York exchange rate for British pounds opened this morning at $5.03625, up 125 from yesterday's close. Later, it fell to $5.0325, which is the latest price.

▲US-France: The New York exchange rate for French francs opened at 6.59 and one-half, down one-eighth from yesterday's close.

▲UK-US: The London foreign exchange market was quiet this morning. The opening price of the UK-US exchange rate was the same as yesterday's closing price of the US-UK exchange rate, remaining $5.035. At 11:00 AM, it rose by 0.0625 to $5.035625. This price did not change at the close.

▲UK-France: The opening price was 76 francs 34, the same as yesterday's closing price. At 11:00, it rose by six pounds to 76 francs 40, and there were no changes afterward.

Cotton and Wheat

▲US Cotton: The cotton market opened slightly higher because Liverpool's telegrams saw the previous market as stable, and the weather in Texas remained dry. The price difference between the July contract and subsequent futures contracts is large, so there is a greater trend in the market today to buy the July contract and sell the distant contract.

▲UK Cotton: The Liverpool cotton market closed down two pounds today for the July contract, at 6.44.

▲UK Wheat: The Liverpool wheat market closed at 4 shillings and 8 pence and 625 today for the July contract, up 875 from yesterday's close.

▲Indian Cotton: Speculators and European merchants are buying in the Bombay cotton market. The closing price of the April-May contract for Jiroji cotton is 216 rupees, up one and a half rupees.

Rubber

▲London Rubber Market: The London rubber market was quiet and stable this afternoon. The trading price for the July and September contracts was 6 pence and 625, the same as yesterday's closing price.

Securities

▲New York Securities: The opening of New York securities was mixed and narrow. Although buying occasionally broke out, stock prices may not rise sustainably until the commercial climate is not clear and the candidates for the executive committee of the Securities Exchange Management Act are not announced. Lloyd George Admonishes the British People Not to Forget Their Important Mission, Establishing Policies to Regain War Opportunities, and His Aspirations Should Extend to Asia

(London) Today, former British Prime Minister Lloyd George, with fiery enthusiasm, published an open letter in the "Viewpoint Report," calling on the British nation not to forget its privileged position in history, but to think about how to fulfill its traditional mission in the international political arena. George stated that the British people seem to have forgotten their previous lofty ideals recently, but with a major disaster looming in Europe today, if we want to turn misfortune into good fortune, the British people must restore their previous strong and fair policies. Since America's hands and feet are bound by its internal disputes, England must rebuild its historical mission today and establish a firm, clear, and easy-to-understand European policy, so that the imminent war can be avoided. George also stated that France has never understood the non-partisan and detached attitude of Britain, and it has sometimes been misunderstood as a contempt for Anglo-French friendship. However, "We joined the European war previously not because of our pro-French sentiment, nor because we were anti-German. Our declaration of war on Germany was only because the balance of power in the world had been harmed by the German-French in 1914, just as the balance of power in Europe was harmed by France in the 18th and 19th centuries. We must follow the mission given to us by history. We have repeatedly saved the freedom of Europe in the past, but today our ambition cannot be limited to Europe alone, but should extend our compassionate attitude to Asia. Isolation is a serious step that humiliates our dignified history." George went on to point out two major mistakes in recent British policy: (1) All signatories to the Treaty of Versailles, whether German or French, should abide by their obligations, especially the reduction of armaments. This article was overlooked. (2) The attitude towards Japan is weak and painful, so that the prestige of the League of Nations has been plunged into eternal ruin. George also stated that on the day a new war breaks out in the future, British intervention can predetermine the fate of the war. Whoever Britain is with will win the final victory. Previously, British politicians did not know how to use this fact, so that Britain's prestige in the international political arena has been reduced to the lowest limit today. George concluded by saying that in today's world, the importance of politicians such as Litvinov, Mussolini, Hitler, and even Barthou has far exceeded that of the past, but the cards in each person's hands cannot be compared with those held by Britain. (22nd National Electric Dispatch)

US-Japan Aircraft Formation: Competing in Long-Distance Flights; One to Alaska, One to Wake Island; Soviet Russia Accumulates Provisions, Preparing for Events in the Far East

(Washington) The War Department announced today that the Air Force will conduct a flight from Washington to Alaska in early July to demonstrate its strength, dispelling external rumors that it is too weak to handle airmail services. The War Department stated that ten giant Martin-type bombers, crewed by twenty Air Force officers and ten enlisted men, will fly to the northernmost territory of the United States. The flight commander is Major Arnold. The exact date of the formation flight has not yet been determined. The War Department noted that the ten giant bombers participating in the early July flight will take off from Bolling Field here, first landing in Minneapolis, then flying across the Canadian border from Minnesota, stopping in Lequin. Subsequent stops include Edmonton, Prince George, Whitehorse, Fairbanks, and Nome. The War Department stated that the purpose of this flight is for training and photography. However, well-informed sources claim that the purpose of this large-scale flight is to wash away the shame of the Air Force's inability to handle airmail services after the government canceled airmail contracts. Since the Air Force took over airmail services, a total of twelve pilots have died in accidents in a short period, with many more seriously injured. There were even days with as many as four pilot fatalities. As a result, national airmail services had to be temporarily suspended for forty-eight hours. Congress has been particularly critical of the Air Force's accidents. It is understood that another purpose of this flight is to visit various cities in Canada to demonstrate the friendship between the two countries. (National Telegram, 21st)

(Tokyo) As the Japanese navy enhances its fleet, the air corps must also be enhanced. Therefore, efforts are underway to train a formation flight of five or six Type 91 monoplanes from Oppama to Sapan Island in the South Seas, a non-stop long-distance flight of 1,300 nautical miles, from the end of July to August. This action was stimulated by the US Air Force’s formation flight held in January of this year and its planned flight for this summer. (Dentsu Telegram, 23rd)

(Tokyo) According to Naval Ministry sources, six light bombers belonging to the Yokosuka Naval Air Corps are scheduled to fly to Sapan Island, one of the Japanese mandated islands in the South Seas, in early July, a distance of 1,300 kilometers. The success of this long-distance flight exercise is closely related to the operations of Japanese naval aircraft in the South Pacific. All sectors in Japan are paying close attention to its results. (Hualian Telegram, 23rd)

(Tokyo) According to another Naval Ministry source, the Japanese Navy is scheduled to hold a large-scale submarine maneuver in the South Seas mandated islands from late July to late August to test the value of the islands in naval warfare. Furthermore, the six naval aircraft that will fly to Sapan Island beforehand will also participate in the exercise. (Hualian Telegram, 23rd)

(Moscow) The People's Committee decided today to actively procure a large number of agricultural machines to harvest Soviet Russia's grain. The Committee ordered the Heavy Industry Committee to take responsibility for procuring the machines and stated firmly that these machines should be delivered on time to support agricultural activities. The Committee's order confirms the predictions previously published by the Associated Press that Soviet Russia's wheat crop may have an astonishingly large harvest this year. The purpose is not only to prepare for war in the Far East but also to engage in dumping on the international market. The order stipulates that Soviet factories should produce 6,475 various machines, 4,000 automatic grain binders, 500 horsepower grain binders, and 7,150 threshing machines of three types by July 15. (National Telegram, 23rd)

Disagreement over Japan's Request to Change Naval Ratio; Great Britain and the United States are Largely in Agreement; US Diplomatic Circles Strongly Urge British Naval Leaders to Suggest Extending the Existing Treaty to Japan

(Washington) According to several observers here today, US diplomatic circles are currently strongly urging British naval leaders to suggest extending the existing treaty and maintaining the original 5:5:3 naval ratio. The US Congressional approval of the strongest navy bill and Great Britain's request to build more cruisers and auxiliary ships both have the power to make Japan accept the existing ratio and no longer demand increases. However, the observers believe that this kind of diplomatic effort may not have any effect. Japan is willing to compromise on all other points, but it insists on naval equality, believing that it is related to Japan's face and national defense. While Great Britain and the United States have many differences of opinion regarding the 1925 naval conference, they both believe that Japan's demand for equality cannot be allowed. (National Telegram, 22nd)

Anglo-American Negotiations Temporarily Suspended; Awaiting US Response to British Request

(London) According to Tokyo news today, Japanese newspapers claim that if Japan does not obtain a modification of the 5:5:3 ratio in next year's naval conference, Japan will announce the abolition of the London Naval Treaty and the Washington Naval Treaty and then independently pursue its naval program for national defense purposes. British and American naval circles are deeply worried upon hearing this threat. It is heard that Japan now opposes the suspension of the naval conference. It is also heard that Foreign Minister Hirota has told the Cabinet that Japan will oppose holding the naval conference in Geneva. It is heard that Japan's opposition to the Soviet Union's participation in the naval conference is not as strong as before. Japan is particularly willing to discuss the issue of Russia, Germany, and Spain attending the conference from a European perspective. Reuters' diplomatic correspondent in London learned today that if Japan raises its demand for naval equality in the current preliminary naval negotiations, the United States may indicate that this would make any naval conference difficult to hold. At the same time, the preliminary naval negotiations between the British and American delegations have been temporarily suspended, awaiting Washington's response to Great Britain's recent request. It is heard that Great Britain's request includes building a large number of small cruisers and aircraft. American experts are currently studying this request and successively reporting the results to Washington. The US Naval Department can probably review the matter and prepare a response next week. (Reuters Telegram, 22nd)

(Tokyo) The US side, at the Anglo-American experts' meeting held in London in preparation for disarmament negotiations, proposed increasing the total tonnage and seeking a total of seventy cruisers, and also had to build a large number of destroyers and new aircraft carriers, which surprised the United States, and Prime Minister MacDonald of Great Britain was in temporary need of travel and rest due to eye disease, so the future of the meeting was already bleak, and the Japanese naval authorities' observations on the future of the meeting and the Anglo-American attitude are as follows: This is an Anglo-American diplomatic battle, and it is difficult to judge future developments without carefully observing future expressions. However, the fact that the meeting has already hit the initial snag is a fact. The UK Navy's request this time is a return to the tough stance around the Geneva Tripartite Conference in 1927, so if this is a genuine claim, the Anglo-American consultation will inevitably lead to a breakdown, and if either the UK or the US does not give way, next year's disarmament conference will of course break down. (Dentsu News Agency Telegram, 23rd)

(New York) According to a Washington dispatch from the New York Times today, Davis, the US representative participating in the Anglo-American naval talks, has notified the State Department that Great Britain is now proposing to build a larger navy. Secretary of State Hull stated that the discussion of this proposal is only exploratory. The dispatch also stated that the State Department is quite surprised that Great Britain made this proposal so quickly in the early stages of the talks, as the State Department initially believed that there would be no substantial developments from London for several weeks or months. There is now an impression of disappointment here, fearing that Great Britain's demand for a larger navy will encourage Japan to demand an expansion of its fleet. If it is said that Great Britain's move may make Japan aware of the price of demanding equality and dare not easily demand equality, then the opposite may be true. (Reuters Telegram, 23rd)

Second Meeting between US and Japan

(London) Japanese Ambassador to Great Britain Matsudaira visited Davis, the chief US representative to the naval conference preparatory talks, this morning to discuss the issues that the US and Japan will raise in the upcoming naval talks. Davis also explained to Ambassador Matsudaira the progress of his recent exchange of views with the British representatives. (Havas, 22nd)

(Washington) According to generally well-informed sources, Japan seems likely to demand the most broadly defined right to naval equality. In other words, Japan intends to make its naval power surpass the navies of all other countries in the Pacific. This point alone may be enough to cause the naval conference to stall. (Havas Telegram, 22nd)

Japan Wants to Divide the World into Three Spheres of Influence; Italian Newspaper Opposes

Foreign newspapers in Rome have reported that Japan seems to have suggested to Great Britain and the United States that the world's oceans be divided into three spheres of influence, with each country having the right and obligation to maintain world peace within its sphere of influence. This news is considered credible here. The "Labor Newspaper" of the Pan-Nationalist Party strongly opposes Japan's request. It stated, "Based on what treaty does Japan want to divide a sphere of influence in the world and assume responsibility for maintaining peace? Japan's intention is to conclude treaties to divide Great Britain and the United States in order to prevent the two countries from reaching an agreement. If Great Britain and the United States could have reached an agreement between 1931 and 1932, then 'Manchukuo' could not have been established. In short, Japan's priority is to continue developing safely towards the Asian continent." The Labor Newspaper also stated that Italy cannot recognize the division of countries into ocean nations and Mediterranean nations. Italy builds ships for navigation on all seven oceans of the world and cannot limit its activities to the Mediterranean alone. (Havas Telegram, 22nd)

Japan Will Build a Large Airfield in Fukuoka; Director of Aviation Bureau Kataoka Completes Survey, Considers it a Key Point for the South Seas and China Routes

Osaka According to the Tobo News, Kataoka Naomichi, Director of the Aviation Bureau of the Ministry of Communications, surveyed the new airfield near Fukuoka City from the 14th to the 21st of this month. After completing the survey, he went to southern Kyushu. According to Kataoka, Fukuoka has major military industry centers such as the Yawata Steel Works, so Fukuoka must have a fully equipped airfield to defend key points and Fukuoka City. In terms of air traffic, Fukuoka will be a key point for aviation to Korea, Taiwan, the South Seas, and the Chinese mainland. Its importance will gradually increase. The Ministry of Communications wants to consult with the Ministry of the Army and sacrifice everything to build an excellent airfield as soon as possible. (Hualian Telegram, 23rd)

France's Second Batch of Shipbuilding

(Paris) Today, the Finance Committee of the Chamber of Deputies passed a draft law authorizing the government to begin construction of a new armored cruiser of the "Dunkerque" class, and one each of submarines and torpedo boats, with a total tonnage of less than 40,000 tons. This is the second batch of shipbuilding program for 1933. According to this case, the Minister of the Navy, Pietri, attended the Finance Committee of the Chamber of Deputies on the 5th of this month to explain it. (Havas Telegram, 22nd)

French Foreign Minister Visits Yugoslavia

Bucharest During his stay here, French Foreign Minister Barthou left for the capital of Yugoslavia this afternoon. Those around the French Foreign Minister believe that this visit to Romania was very successful. Upon departure, the French Foreign Minister declared to the press that his views and those of the Romanian Prime Minister were completely consistent (National Telegram, 23rd)

Bucharest, Romania King Carol received French journalists at the palace and made the following remarks: "The French Foreign Minister Barthou made a special trip to this country. I took this opportunity to reaffirm the friendship between the two countries and am very pleased. Romania not only has friendship with France but also deep affection. The hospitality extended to the French Foreign Minister here is sincere and cannot be compared to ordinary diplomatic courtesies. Our people have deep sympathy for France, and the long-standing relations between the two countries have always been based on emotion and intelligence. I deeply pray that this visit by the French diplomatic representative will further benefit and strengthen these relations." (Havas Telegram, 22nd)

MacDonald's Three-Month Vacation; Plans for a Tour of South America

(London) According to reliable sources today, Prime Minister MacDonald plans to travel to South America with his daughter for a tour of the Amazon River. An ophthalmologist advised MacDonald to take a three-month vacation to avoid overusing his eyes. However, the date of the Prime Minister's departure has not yet been determined (National Telegram, 23rd)

International Labor Bureau; China Elected as Director; General Assembly Passes Invitation to US to Participate; Cheering Resounds Throughout the Venue

(Geneva) This morning, at the International Labor Conference, China was elected as a director of the International Labor Bureau with sixty votes for a term of three years. (Central News Agency Telegram, 23rd)

(Geneva) China, Argentina, Brazil, and Mexico were elected today as administrators of the International Labor Bureau. One condition for Mexico's election is that if the United States joins the Labor Bureau, Mexico will cede this seat to the United States. However, unofficial news from Washington claims that the United States will join the International Labor Bureau, but not at this session (National Telegram, 25th)

(Geneva) Today, the International Labor Conference unanimously passed a resolution, which was immediately telegraphed to Washington, expressing warm welcome for the US Congress's passage of a bill authorizing President Roosevelt to declare accession to the International Labor Organization. (Note: This bill has been signed by the President, and Congress simultaneously declared that the United States cannot bear any obligations under the League of Nations Covenant by joining the International Labor Organization.) The US representatives, who previously attended the conference as observers, formally attended today, and applause from the delegates of various countries lasted for a long time. US government representative Gann, employer representative Antwees, and labor representative Lewis spoke successively, expressing their gratitude for the conference's warm reception, saying that once the government grants them authority, they will wholeheartedly assist in the progress of the conference. Labor representative Lewis, on behalf of William Green, President of the American Federation of Labor, also invited the Director of the International Labor Bureau, Butler, to go to San Francisco in October to attend the American Federation of Labor Convention and deliver a speech. (Havas Telegram, 22nd)

Turkey Increases Military Spending

Ankara The Turkish government decided today to increase military spending from 40 million Turkish pounds to 60 million Turkish pounds. Last year's total national expenditure was 170 million Turkish pounds, and the Turkish people's burden of direct taxes alone accounted for 45% of the total expenditure. Therefore, this increase in military spending is noteworthy. (National Telegram, 22nd)

Afghanistan and Colombia; Japan Establishes Embassies

(Tokyo) In light of the recent serious international situation, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has decided to establish new embassies in Colombia in South America and Afghanistan in Asia Minor. It has decided to appoint Iwate Yoshio, the current Counselor in Italy, as the Minister to Colombia, and Kitada Tadashi, the Consul-General in Alexandria, as the Minister to Afghanistan. Both will begin their duties on July 1st. (Nichiren Telegram, 23rd)

British Crown Prince, Approaching Forty, Still Single; Lifelong Passion for Golf

(London) Today is the British Crown Prince's fortieth birthday, and congratulations have poured in from all sides. However, the Crown Prince has reached middle age, and the issue of marriage is still shelved. No one in the palace is talking about it, and even Cupid is helpless. The Crown Prince himself is still carefree as ever. His greatest passion is golf. Next Tuesday, he plans to visit Southampton to watch the British-American golf finals (National Telegram, 13th)
