Chen Guoxiang, Zhou Shengfa, and others who accompanied him have not yet returned to Songjiang.

Suzhou: Garment Workers Cause More Disturbances

Since the strike in the garment industry in Wu County, the county party headquarters considered the industry's trade association to be poorly organized and ordered it to cease activities. On the afternoon of the 22nd, at 4:00 PM, it convened a meeting of members. Unexpectedly, some non-members misunderstood, and more than a hundred workers went to the county party headquarters. Led by Fan Jiqing, Teng Yuanquan, and others, they made two requests to the party headquarters: (1) Remove all existing personnel from the trade association; (2) When the trade association is reorganized, the name must be changed to the Garment Workers Association. After an explanation by Secretary Xu, they withdrew. At that time, six representatives from the trade association, including Lu Chunjiang, were present. After a conversation with Standing Committee Member Zhu, they withdrew. Unexpectedly, as soon as they left the gate, the six representatives were surrounded by workers. Lu Chunjiang and Cai Heshang were seized and taken to Xuanyuan Hall. Xiao, the police officer in charge of the police district, ordered Lu, Cai, and Teng Yuanquan to return. Lu and Cai provided surety and were released.

Jiading: Guangdong Man Comes to Jiading to Commit Suicide

On the afternoon of the 22nd, a young man in a Western suit arrived at Wangxianqiao Town in the western countryside and hired a Jiangbei pontoon boat to Suzhou, saying that the boat fare was five yuan. The townspeople found it strange that he did not take the train but hired a small boat that was not suitable in terms of time and money. When asked about his background, he gave evasive answers. Later, the young man took out a security razor in a small teahouse and slashed his throat to commit suicide. He was stopped, but his throat had already been cut open for more than two inches, and blood was gushing, staining his chest and abdomen. Wu Zongqi, the town mayor, quickly bandaged him and reported the incident to the Wai Gang Public Security Substation, which ordered the police to meet and take him to the station. According to Xie Bin, from Taishan County, Guangdong, unemployed, he committed suicide because he was addicted to opium and let down his friends. A business card found on him was engraved with Xie Yunwu, a graduate of Meiji University in Japan, Xie Chen, Xie Langchen, etc. It is not known which name is correct. He also had a letter addressed to Cui Youyu in Huanglongdong, Songmutiang, Hangzhou, which read: "Xie Junxiong is going to Hangzhou to avoid misfortune and plans to stay with you for a short time. Please provide accommodation. Sincerely, Guan Tingbin." It appeared that Guan had introduced him to Cui. There was also a diary with contact information for friends, including Lu Jiawang at No. 18, Wu Fang, Ximen Road, Shanghai, He Yiming, Deputy Adjutant of the Suzhou Tax Police Regiment, and Guan Chongbi, Chief of the Jiangsu Wuxi Station Police Section. A document was immediately prepared and sent to the county government through the County Public Security Bureau. County Magistrate Xu ordered him to be sent to Jiading Hospital. Dr. Geng Shiting examined him and found that the trachea and esophagus were not broken. When asked for his real name, he did not answer, saying only that life was meaningless because he was too distressed. When asked again, he claimed to be mentally disturbed and refused to reveal anything. After treatment, he was asked to leave the hospital. When they insisted on keeping him, he struggled and ran out. He was ordered to track him down and hand him over to the Public Security Bureau to have his friends claim him to avoid further accidents.

Wujiang: Counterfeit Money Found at Bus Station

The bicycle team of the County Public Security Bureau discovered two criminals, Liu Pinshan and He Yunhui, at the Suzhou-Jiahe Road bus station, who were using counterfeit money from the Central Bank to make purchases at Shengjia Store, Wu Xiangxing, Tongrenhe, Shangjielu and other shops in the city. A large amount of counterfeit money and real money was confiscated on the spot and sent to the County Government. After a court hearing, Liu and He were each fined 300 yuan, but the source of the counterfeit money was not investigated. It is now heard that the shops, considering the county government's sentence too lenient, have jointly requested the county chamber of commerce to send a telegram to the Central Bank, ordering the county to investigate the case to serve as a warning.

Wuxi: Husband Has an Affair, Wife Attempts Suicide

Chen Jinnian, a 35-year-old accountant at Taichang Shipping Bureau under Gongyun Bridge in this city, married Guo Hongying and has a son, four years old. The couple had a harmonious relationship, but Jinnian was fond of women. Last winter, he became acquainted with Jin Aizhen, a romantic young woman. When Hongying learned of the affair, conflicts arose. In her anger, Guo repeatedly attempted suicide, more than fifteen times. Recently, she jumped into the river under Gongyun Bridge, but was rescued and did not die. The day before yesterday, Guo, taking advantage of Jinnian's absence, privately purchased raw opium at her residence at No. 4 Wangren Lane and swallowed it to commit suicide. She groaned in bed. Li, who lived with her, heard the noise, knew something was wrong, immediately opened the door and entered the room. She saw Guo's face pale, lying stiffly on the bed, tears in her eyes. Knowing she had taken poison, she immediately sent Guo to Dr. Zhang Jimin's clinic under Tonghui Bridge for two life-saving injections, and then transferred her to the Brothers Hospital for treatment. Her life is now out of danger.

Search for Red Pills Sparks Repercussions

Since the establishment of the County Anti-Smoking Bureau, the investigation section chief has been Chen Yuchu, the original member of the Public Security Bureau and Anti-Smoking Committee. In recent days, the Public Security Bureau's Inspectorate and various branches have been diligently searching, with more than a dozen cases every day. The various red pill dens and "swallow nests" (opium dens) are facing their doom. Yesterday, at 6:30 AM, as soon as the Li Wansheng Candle Shop outside the North Gate, in Tantou Lane, opened, more than 30 armed patrolmen from the Public Security Bureau Inspectorate suddenly spread out as sentries, prohibiting traffic and searching the shop for red pills. They searched the shop, dormitory, and kitchen, thoroughly searching every corner. As a result, they found nothing and left in disappointment. Afterwards, the shop felt that it had been searched for no reason and feared that it would encourage false accusations and framing. The trade association requested the county government to strictly investigate the reporter to maintain the market and social order. The shop is opened by a Ningbo native, Shen. Therefore, Wu Zhihe, chairman of the Ning Shao Fellow Association, personally requested Chen, the director of the Public Security Bureau, to thoroughly investigate the truth. At the same time, Qian Sunqing, Li Tiping, and Cheng Jingtang, members of the County Anti-Smoking Committee, also sent a letter to Chairman Yan requesting to temporarily postpone the large-scale inspections before the official ointment shop opens and smokers register and receive permits to avoid disturbance and maintain order.

County Land Bureau Established

The Wuxi County Land Bureau Preparatory Office has been established for more than half a year. Recently, the preparatory work has been completed, and the declaration of land prices is about to begin. Hu Pinfang, director of the preparatory office, prepared a report and submitted it to the provincial government for the establishment of the Land Bureau. It has now been approved. Hu Pinfang was appointed as the director, and the bureau was established immediately to actively handle land declarations.

Changzhou: High School Student Entrance Exam Concludes

The graduation examination for high school students in Jiangsu Province was held in districts, dividing the province into nine districts. Wujin belonged to the second district. The examiner was Wang Delin, editor of the Education Department, and the supervisors were Cai Pei, Wujin County Magistrate, and Qian Hao, Director of the Education Bureau. The examination was held upstairs in the auditorium of the Provincial Changzhou High School. A total of 49 students from Provincial Changzhou High School and 22 students from Private Changzhou High School participated in the examination. On the morning of June 20, they took the Chinese Language test, and in the afternoon, the Party Principles and History tests. On the morning of the 21st, they took the Mathematics test, and in the afternoon, the Geography test. On the morning of the 22nd, they took the English test, and in the afternoon, the Physics test. On the morning of the 23rd, they took the Chemistry test, and in the afternoon, the Biology test. After today (23rd), the examiner will take the exam papers to the Education Department to evaluate the quality and determine whether the students will graduate.

Jiangyin: Protection Corps Temporarily Postponed Reorganization

County Magistrate Bao, according to the order of the Provincial Security Office, ordered the existing temporary protection corps and police team to be merged into a protection team. However, Jiangyin had no temporary protection organization. In addition to reorganizing the original police team's squadron and independent detachment into the first squadron of the protection team, more than a thousand volunteer members of other protection corps, with more than 1,470 firearms, should be handled. Also, how should the expenses of the original police team, one squadron, and one independent detachment be offset against the expenses of the reorganized first squadron, which is insufficient? Furthermore, should the protection corps headquarters follow the organizational chart issued by the province and reduce expenses? The decision was made at the political affairs meeting on the 21st: (1) The police force in this county is weak and relies on volunteer members of the protection corps to defend the peace. The security of each township can be maintained. All firearms are also purchased by donations from various places. How should they be organized? The general headquarters of the county protection corps will discuss the measures and submit them to the Security Office for approval. (2) The regular expenses of the original police team, one squadron, and one independent detachment, will be reorganized into the first squadron according to the measures issued by the province. The incidental expenses will still be distributed according to the original amount. (3) The expenses of the protection corps in this county have not yet been determined. The general headquarters of the protection corps will postpone the reorganization.

District, Township, and Town Boundaries Confirmed

The Civil Affairs Department ordered the county to reorganize the district, township, and town boundaries. The county government has reduced the 14 districts in the county to 7 districts. Li Dichen and others, the heads of the 7 districts, were also appointed by the county and approved by the Civil Affairs Department. The implementation will begin on July 1. The standards for the distribution of autonomous funds for districts, townships, and towns are as follows: (A) District Office expenses: (1) Grade A: Districts with a population of more than 100,000 (3 districts), each district receives 200 yuan per month; (2) Grade B: Districts with a population of less than 100,000 (4 districts), each district receives 100 yuan per month; (B) Township and Town Office expenses: (1) Grade A: Townships and towns with a population of more than 6,000 (36 townships and towns), each township and town receives 12 yuan per month; (2) Grade B: Townships and towns with a population of less than 6,000 (92 townships and towns), each township and town receives 10 yuan per month.

Zhenjiang: Sexagenarian Commits Suicide Due to Unemployment

Yao Changsheng from Suzhou, nearly sixty years old, used to be a guard in the Suzhou Security Corps. Later, he was dismissed due to an incident. He came to Zhenjiang to seek employment and lived at No. 6, Niunaifang, Xi Chengwai, Jingji Ridge, the home of his nephew Yao Guoxi. He repeatedly asked friends for recommendations. Unexpectedly, he lived there for several years without finding a place to settle down and was very depressed. Yesterday, he said to his nephew, "I am going to Baogai Mountain to talk to a friend," and then went out. He did not return by lunchtime. Guoxi was suspicious. When he did not return by dinner, Guoxi was even more surprised. He went to the homes of various friends to inquire and learned that he had borrowed one yuan from a friend and purchased raw opium to swallow. Guoxi was shocked and led people to Baogai Mountain to find him. He found his uncle lying on the grass, barely breathing. He immediately hired a cart and sent him to the hospital for treatment. Because it was too late, the operation was ineffective. His life is in danger.

Yangzhou Qingzhen Car Implements Allied Forces

Since the completion and opening of the Yang Qing Highway, the Highway Bureau has been actively preparing for joint transportation. However, one bridge in Shaobo has not yet been completed. Therefore, the section from Yangzhou to Shaobo still requires a boat ride. Yesterday, Shen, the director of the Highway Administration, Zhu Ganchen, the coordinator of the Zhen Yang Automobile Company, and Yang Peisun, an employee, signed a joint transportation contract in the Construction Hall. The sale of joint transportation tickets will begin today. There will be one long-distance bus and two short-distance buses running in each direction every day. The bus will depart from Zhenjiang at 7:00 AM and arrive in Pukou at 4:00 PM. The departure times and passenger fares are listed below: (Departure times) Upstream: Zhenjiang bus departs at 6:40 AM, arrives in Yangzhou at 7:40 AM. Yangzhou ferry departs at 8:00 AM, arrives in Shaobo at 9:20 AM. Shaobo bus departs at 9:30 AM, arrives in Qingjiang at 3:00 PM (resting for half an hour in Gaoyou for passengers to have lunch). Downstream: Qingjiang bus departs at 7:00 AM, arrives in Shaobo at 12:20 PM (resting for half an hour in Gaoyou for passengers to have lunch). Shaobo ferry departs at 12:40 PM, arrives in Yangzhou at 1:40 PM. Yangzhou bus departs at 2:00 PM, arrives in Zhenjiang at 3:00 PM. (Passenger fares) Zhenjiang to Qingjiangpu, 4 yuan 35 cents. Yangzhou to Qingjiangpu, 3 yuan 35 cents. Joint transportation buses do not have half-price tickets for military police.

Nantong: Jiangsu North-South Telephone Project

The Jiangsu Long-Distance Telephone Administration of the Ministry of Communications, in order to connect the telephones in the north and south of Jiangsu, is laying submarine cables between Jiangyin and Jingjiang. The laying of cables from Nantong to Jingjiang began on the 13th, and then from Jingjiang to Wuxi. It is expected to be completed in two months. Direct telephone communication will be possible throughout the province.

Dispute After Military Judge's Death

Qu Yaodong, a native of this city, served as a military judge in the Wei Lihuang Eastern Route Army Frontline Headquarters. He traveled to northern Fujian, but due to acclimatization, he returned home sick. Due to the fatigue of the journey, he passed away. On the day of the funeral, his ex-wife, Xing Dezhi, who was already divorced, suddenly returned home and argued with Qu's wife, Wu Yongcheng, over the mourning clothes and jumped into the coffin, causing a great commotion. Wu Yongcheng filed a complaint with the court against Xing on the 22nd. Xing was summoned by the criminal court but did not appear. The summons will continue to be issued.

Gaoyou: Tragedy of Bomb Explosion

In Xinglong'an, Houhezhen in the tenth district of this county, six blacksmiths from Funing have been making wheat sickles and farm tools since last month. Their business is quite good. The day before yesterday, due to a shortage of raw materials, they went to Xinghua to purchase a boatload of scrap iron. Yesterday, they picked out three iron balls similar to weighing hammers and put them into the furnace to forge. Unexpectedly, a moment after entering the furnace, they suddenly exploded with a loud noise. The anvil flew with the sound, killing three blacksmiths. Two had their arms broken, and one had his head blown off. Blood and flesh flew everywhere. The blacksmith owner, Mao, prepared coffins, collected the bodies, and transported them back to his hometown.

Tenth District Plagued by Locusts

The area of Xiajiaji and Zhoujin Township in the tenth district of the county has recently experienced dry weather. Locusts have been found covering the fields and gnawing on rice seedlings, causing great damage. Although the locust control officers of each township have worked hard to catch and kill them, there are too many locusts, making it difficult to eliminate them. If it does not rain again, once the locusts take flight, a locust plague will be inevitable.

Haimen: Rascal Attempts Rape, Commits Assault

Wang, the wife of farmer Huang Laoer in Rixin Township, third district, is over thirty years old and has a bit of beauty. Yesterday (21st) at dusk, Huang went out due to business. Suddenly, a rascal, Lu Bao San, broke into the room, grabbed Wang, and pressed her to the ground, intending to rape her. Wang screamed for help. Lu, failing to get what he wanted, took a kitchen knife and slashed Wang's left leg twice, causing blood to flow like a river and seriously injuring her. When neighbors heard the sound and came over, Lu had already fled. Today (22nd), Huang has filed a complaint with the county government for investigation and handling.

Arsonist Burns Two Children to Death

Lu Xiaolin, a farmer in Letong Township, sixth district, is of modest means. He had a long-standing feud with Wang, who lived nearby. The day before yesterday (20th) at midnight, Wang set fire to Lu's thatched house. In an instant, thick smoke filled the air, and flames soared. Lu was awakened from his dream and rang the gong to call for help. However, the weather was dry and the wind was strong, making it difficult to stop the fire. The five thatched houses and belongings were all reduced to ashes. Lu's wife, Chen, was injured on the head while fleeing in a hurry. A one-year-old boy and a five-year-old girl were unable to escape and were buried in the fire. It was a tragedy.

Ningbo: Hundreds of Road Workers Fight Villagers

The Ningchuan Highway has been under construction for more than a year. Most of the road construction has been completed and is scheduled to open to traffic on the first day of next month. However, the section in Shanmen Township, sixth district of Zhenhai, has not yet been completed. Therefore, the company recently sent many workers to the area to rush construction. Wang Ruilin and other contractors will be able to complete the work soon. The day before yesterday, a resident, Shi Yanchang, and others, for some unknown reason, had an argument with the road workers. Then, both sides gathered their accomplices and engaged in hand-to-hand combat. More than a hundred road workers, lacking weapons, swarmed to Xiapu and looted all the meat cleavers from the meat shops in the market as weapons. The order was disrupted for a time and could not be restored. Fortunately, the military and police nearby heard the news and sent a team to disperse the road workers, and the matter was settled. However, villagers Ni Xiaoliu, Zhang Biao, Shi Yanchang, Chen Er, etc., were all seriously injured and taken away by the road workers. Their fate is uncertain. The military and police agencies are currently investigating the perpetrators and rescuing the abducted villagers.

Xiaoshan: Southern Qianqing Bandits Rob Night Boat

The Xiaoshan Xixing Cao'e night boat, sailing to Southern Qianqing on the night of the 21st, suddenly encountered a bandit boat. More than ten bandits boarded the boat and looted wildly, taking more than seventy yuan of silver dollars and clothing worth more than a hundred yuan from the passengers. Also, two foreign letters on the boat, worth more than thirty yuan, and four bolts of silk, worth more than two hundred yuan, were also taken. The boatman, A Gui, was stabbed in five places by a bandit's knife, but fortunately, none of the wounds were fatal, and his life is not in danger. The boatman has reported the incident to the maritime and land public security agencies of Shao and Xiao counties for joint investigation.

Murder Case Occurs in Qidu Mountain

A farmer, Zhu Ayuan, at the foot of Qidu Mountain in southern Xiaoshan, had a dispute with a neighbor over a field ridge. On the 20th, Ayuan led the neighbor's cow back home and killed it. The neighbor, surnamed Zhang, learned of this and gathered more than ten people to destroy Zhu's house and stabbed Ayuan five times in vital areas, killing him on the spot. Ayuan's five-year-old son was thrown into a dung pit and drowned. The whole village is now outraged and has reported the incident to the provincial and county authorities, requesting that the perpetrators be severely punished to maintain local peace. It is unknown how this murder case will be resolved.

Letter from Henan Evening News

Dear Editor,

We have read the news article "Head-Shaking Case Judgement" published in your newspaper on June 15, which is quite different from the facts. This case was judged in Zheng County Court on May 14, and the original judgment has been revoked. There is no word "one month" in the judgment. This is a matter of honor and disgrace for the entire journalism community. Please correct it. Thank you very much.

Sincerely,

Henan Evening News

Local News

Chairman Chiang Kai-shek Will Not Come to Shanghai, Will Go Directly to Hangzhou from Nanjing Tomorrow, Whether to Return to Fenghua Will Be Decided After Arriving in Hangzhou

Xin Xin News Agency: Regarding the news that Chairman Chiang Kai-shek of the Military Affairs Commission will come to Shanghai, Song Ziwen, a standing committee member of the National Economic Commission, told Xin Xin News Agency reporters yesterday that Chiang is scheduled to leave Nanjing tomorrow (today) and go directly to Hangzhou to inspect the highways of five provinces. He will not come to Shanghai. As for whether he will return to his ancestral home in Fenghua, it is said that the decision will be made after arriving in Hangzhou. It is also learned that Chiang Kai-shek's departure from Nanjing will be at the earliest this afternoon, as Chiang is scheduled to give a speech to the Central Military Academy this morning.

Song Ziwen Discusses Autumn Trip to Sichuan for Inspection, Establishment of the Construction Bank Corporation Decided for July 1st, China's Silver Import Surplus Not Necessarily Leading to Large-Scale Outflow

Song Ziwen, a standing committee member of the National Economic Council, after convening a standing committee meeting in Beijing, returned to Shanghai by express train from Beijing at around 11:00 PM the night before. At 11:00 AM yesterday, at the NEC office on Rue Amiral de Ham, he met with reporters from various newspapers. The following is a record of his remarks:

Autumn Trip to Sichuan

Mr. Song first stated that his trip to Sichuan for inspection had been decided long ago, but it had to wait until after summer, when the weather cooled down in early autumn, before it could take place. Regarding the organization of the Construction Bank Corporation, it is scheduled to be officially established on July 1st. Internal staff have largely been internally determined. As for which work to start first after its establishment, it still requires detailed planning before it can be carried out.

Rajchman's Return to China

He then said that he had not yet received a telegram from Ludwik Rajchman, the League of Nations technical cooperation liaison to China, regarding when he would return to China. As for the secretary of NEC consultant Monnet, he had another part of his work to do and had to return to the United States. This time, his landing in Japan was purely a transit. It was not a special mission.

Cotton and Wheat Loans

Mr. Song continued to talk about the U.S. cotton and wheat loans. Everything will be in accordance with the amended contract, and it will be paid off within five years according to the contract. Among them, wheat and flour can also be returned in full from the fourth year.

Raising Silver Prices

Then, the reporter asked if the U.S. silver price increase bill had been approved, and whether China's silver would flow out in large quantities. Mr. Song then expressed his opinion, saying that he never believed that China would have a large outflow of silver due to the U.S. silver price increase. He is in contact with the financial community every day, and has not heard that they are very panicked about this. Chinese people often misunderstand that import and export surpluses directly affect the inflow and outflow of silver. In fact, an import surplus does not necessarily cause silver to flow out, because there is often a part of remittances from overseas Chinese.

Bimetallic System

When asked about the opinions of some bankers who advocate the implementation of a bimetallic system to use both gold and silver, Mr. Song replied that many countries have experimented with the implementation of bimetallicism in the past, and the results were not good. What will happen in the future is unpredictable, but China does not have gold. If we implement a bimetallic system, we must first buy cash, which is not necessary at present and is unnecessary.

Gu Ambassador Returns Home

Mr. Song finally said that Mr. Gu Shaochuan (Weijun), the Chinese ambassador to France, is returning to China on his own leave. The reason is that Mr. Gu has requested leave four or five times, and it has only been approved now. The expenses of the Chinese embassy in France are relatively high, and other embassies and consulates also have this difficulty. Finally, when asked about issues such as diplomacy, the opening of traffic and mail in North China, and Huang Shaoxiong's southward journey, Mr. Song replied that he did not know. He said that his trip to Beijing was purely for the discussion of the budget of the Economic Council, and he had not discussed these issues with President Wang and others, so he had nothing to say.

Garrison Headquarters Strictly Prohibits Highly Toxic Drugs, Posts Slogans and Notices to Inform the Public, So as Not to Cause the Public to Accidentally Violate the Law

German Consul General in Shanghai, Mr. Krieb, Speaks, Expressing That He Will Never Recognize the Puppet Manchukuo, German Overseas Chinese Hold Grand Banquet Last Night

The Shen Shi News Agency reports that Mr. Krieb, the new German Consul General in Shanghai, arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday and met with reporters to make a statement. The Shen Shi News Agency reporter specially recorded the details as follows:

Germany Does Not Recognize Puppet Manchukuo

Regarding the previous rumors that Germany would recognize the Puppet Manchukuo, Mr. Krieb first replied to the reporter that regarding the so-called Manchukuo issue, although Germany has now withdrawn from the League of Nations, I firmly believe that Germany will take the same steps as the League of Nations. We will never recognize the Puppet Manchukuo, and we still have considerable obligations to the League of Nations, and there will never be a proposal to recognize the Puppet Manchukuo.

Rejoining the League of Nations Issue

Regarding the issue of Germany rejoining the League of Nations, according to Mr. Krieb, there is currently considerable possibility, but what the German government and people hope is that the League of Nations must respect Germany's opinions, and whether to join in the future will be a prerequisite. As for the recent rumors that Germany will implement an active policy towards China after my arrival in Shanghai, this statement is not true. I dare to assert that Germany is very concerned about the developing Far East issue, but there is no intention to take active action. Although Mr. Hitler is paying attention to the Far East, he is still devoting all his efforts to Europe.

Trend of German-Russian Relations

Mr. Krieb continued to talk about the trend of German-Russian relations improving, saying that the German government sincerely hopes to have friendly relations with Soviet Russia, but the current political organization of Soviet Russia is different from the German political system under Chancellor Hitler. At the same time, there are various other economic reasons that hinder German-Russian friendship. As for the issue of armaments, Germany has its own reasons and will not be willing to make the slightest concession. The political situation in Germany has improved compared to before, and the power of the Communist Party has gradually decreased.

Overseas Chinese Host Banquet for Mr. Krieb

After Mr. Krieb arrived in Shanghai, he visited various major cultural institutions for several days. At 6:00 PM last night, all the overseas Chinese in Germany specially held a grand banquet at the German School at No. 1 Avenue Dubail to welcome Mr. Krieb.

Spring Season This Year, Consolidated Tax Revenue Increases Sharply, Monthly Increases, Most in March, Currently Making Every Effort to Develop, Will Be Comparable to Salt Tax

Since the collection of the consolidated tax on cigarettes in the 17th year of the Republic of China, the Ministry of Finance's Taxation Department has successively handled the consolidated taxes on cotton yarn, wheat flour, matches, cement, flue-cured tobacco, and machine-made wine. In less than seven years, tax revenue has increased annually. A reporter from the New News Agency recently learned from the tax authorities that the Ministry of Finance's Taxation Department is currently making every effort to develop the consolidated tax, and it is expected that it will soon be comparable to the salt tax. In the first quarter of this year, the national consolidated tax revenue increased in each month. It increased by more than 1.6 million yuan in January, more than 2 million yuan in February, and more than 2.7 million yuan in March. The reasons for the increase in revenue are approximately the following three points: (1) Tax increase: Starting from December 5th last year, the tax rates for cigarettes, matches, and cement were increased. Except for the small amount of matches and cement, the cigarette tax increased sharply after the tax increase. (2) The consolidated taxes of Hebei, Jin, Chahar, and Sui provinces were previously handled by the Hebei Special Commissioner's Office of the Ministry of Finance. Except for the cigarette tax, which was paid to the national treasury, all were retained by the Hebei authorities for military and political expenses. Since the establishment of the Hebei, Jin, Chahar, and Sui Regional Bureau in November last year, all consolidated tax revenue has been paid to the treasury. The consolidated tax revenue has therefore increased. (3) The flue-cured tobacco produced in China is very large in Jinan, Bengbu, and Xuchang. In the past, the tax collection method was not perfect, and the amount collected was limited. Recently, it has been vigorously improved and is gradually on the right track, which is also a reason for the increase in tax revenue.

The situation in the tea market has gradually improved.

Green Tea Sold Out

Chinese tea is divided into three categories: black tea, green tea, and tea bricks. Foreigners prefer to buy black tea to quench their thirst due to different preferences. Although green tea has a very clear fragrance, there are very few drinkers. The situation in this year's tea market seems to be particularly different from last year. The Zhenmei and Zhenmei green teas from Tunxi, Shexian, and Suian have been sold out. The foreign demand is very strong, which is really a new record in the tea industry.

The Association Intends to Host People from All Walks of Life to Defend Against the Public Works Bureau's Explanation. Rickshaw Pullers Submit to the Public Works Bureau to Sponsor the Management Committee.

The Shanghai Rickshaw Industry Association Special Zone Office believes that the Rickshaw Management Committee of the Public Works Bureau's proposals to reduce rickshaw fares and improve rickshaw styles are inappropriate. It has requested the Public Works Bureau to abolish the Management Committee to maintain the difficulties of the merchants. At the same time, it will defend against the explanation of the Management Committee. However, the rickshaw puller representatives expressed their support for the Public Works Bureau's handling. The details are as follows:

Periodic Vehicle Inspection and Certificate Issuance

The Rickshaw Industry Association Special Zone Office, dissatisfied with the new regulations and certificate issuance methods of the Rickshaw Management Committee of the Public Works Bureau, established a Registration Committee to conduct its own review and certificate issuance, and stipulated the daily review and certificate issuance period. When issuing certificates, the substitute donor must request proof of the substitute donation number, and then the committee will review and issue the certificate to ensure protection. No. 1 to No. 2000 will be issued from the 29th to July 1st, No. 2001 to No. 4000 will be issued from July 5th to 7th, No. 4001 to No. 5000 will be issued from July 8th to 10th, No. 5001 to No. 6000 will be issued from July 11th to 13th, No. 6001 to No. 7000 will be issued from July 14th to 16th, No. 7001 to No. 8000 will be issued from July 17th to 20th, No. 8001 to No. 9000 will be issued from July 21st to 23rd, and No. 9001 to No. 10000 will be issued from July 21st to 23rd.

Yesterday, the person in charge of the Rickshaw Industry Association Special Zone Office told a reporter from the New News Agency that the Public Works Bureau Rickshaw Management Committee's proposed plans to improve rickshaw styles, help rickshaw pullers, and reduce rickshaw fares did not take into account the interests of the rickshaw owners themselves, and imposed a deadline for applying for certificates as a threat. It has requested the Public Works Bureau to abolish its proposals. The association is scheduled to convene the 34th board of directors meeting at 9:00 PM tonight (last night) to discuss and defend against it. At the same time, it will regularly host people from all walks of life to report the truth to avoid being deceived. The general meeting decided to send representatives to the Public Works Bureau to petition, and plans to go there after hosting people from all walks of life, and strive for the bureau to withdraw its decision to maintain the livelihood of the rickshaw owners.

Rickshaw Pullers Sponsor the Management Committee

According to the Public Works Bureau Information Office, the Public Works Bureau Rickshaw Management Committee recently announced its latest plan, that is, from August 1st of this year, the rickshaw fare will be reduced to 10 cents in small ocean coins, and from January 1st next year, it will be reduced to 8 cents in small ocean coins. In recent days, several rickshaw puller representatives have come to the management office to express their support and request the management office not to be deceived by the rickshaw owners' propaganda. One of the rickshaw puller representatives' submissions is excerpted as follows: The people suffer because a few old rickshaw merchants control the rickshaw business and arbitrarily increase the rickshaw fare to as much as 16 cents. The people work hard all day but find it difficult to get a full meal. The new regulations have been published in newspapers many times, and after that, the rickshaw fare shall not exceed 8 cents per day, which greatly benefits the poor. We are looking forward to its realization every day. Unexpectedly, recently, a few unscrupulous merchants have, in the name of the association, issued declarations, publicly slandering the government's policy of improving rickshaws and helping rickshaw pullers in order to deprive them of their attempts, and decided on three measures: (1) To not recognize the management office, (2) To still have the certificate issuance handled by a few people, not directly, (3) The rickshaw owners shall not freely advocate and must obey them. Tracing their intentions, it is nothing more than a conspiracy to control and monopolize. Improving rickshaws is not only beautiful in appearance, but also suitable for passengers. What are the drawbacks? As for applying for registration, it is to facilitate rickshaw owners to freely obtain certificates and avoid being bound by them. What is the disadvantage for rickshaw owners?

Salaries account for only a small part of the total expenditure. Taking the two Chinese companies in Zhabei as an example, it is only about 8%. Furthermore, the power generation capacity of the two Chinese companies in Zhabei is about one-tenth of that of the Shanghai Electric Power Company. For example, Shanghai Electric Power Company generates electricity and consumes 17.534 BTU. The coal price per million BTU is 0.448 yuan, and Zhabei consumes 22.467 BTU, and the coal price is 0.54 yuan. All other consumption is the same. City Chamber of Commerce Requests Increase in Import Tax on Clocks to Protect Domestic Industry Development

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce submitted a document to the Ministry of Finance yesterday, stating, regarding the matter of requesting a decision, that the chamber held its fifth member conference on June 17th. Based on a proposal from the Clock and Watch and Eyeglasses Guilds, requesting the imposition of an anti-dumping tax on imported clocks or an increase in import duties on clocks, it was stated that clocks are produced abroad, and those engaged in the clock and watch industry are merchants. Since the September 18th Incident, the Chinese people have understood that the way to save the country lies in promoting domestic goods. Enthusiastic members of the industry have invested in establishing clock factories, and their various clock products are sufficient to resist foreign goods and have long been praised by users. However, due to the impact of Japanese dumping, domestic production is at risk of being overwhelmed. According to investigations by clock factories, domestic clocks are currently sufficient to meet the needs of the Chinese people. It is proposed that the conference request the government to impose anti-dumping taxes or increase import duty rates on imported clocks. The benefits of this would be: firstly, to increase national treasury revenue; secondly, to promote domestic goods, achieving two benefits with one action, and so on. This was submitted to the conference for discussion, which recognized that domestic clocks in Tianjin, Shanghai, and Yantai have been manufactured in recent years to be sturdy and practical, not inferior to foreign products. The clocks produced in Tianjin were even displayed at the Railway Line Goods Exhibition, and the impression of domestic clocks has gradually spread throughout society. However, due to their relatively shallow roots, they cannot compete with foreign goods without state protection. The original proposal to impose anti-dumping taxes on imported clocks or increase import duties on clocks was resolved to be forwarded as a record. It is appropriate to record the case and submit a document requesting your ministry to review and approve its implementation for public benefit, etc.

Records of the General Meeting of the Southern District Rice Merchants Association

The Shanghai Southern District Rice Merchants Association convened the rice industry from various inland ports at the Yimiao Cuixiu Hall yesterday for the 16th Annual General Meeting. Representatives from various rice industries who attended the meeting included: Qingpu: Zhu Hongsun, Zhuang Fangsun, Xu Junqing, Feng Peiyu, Jiaoli: Lai Ziqi, Ye Shaoqiu, Shen Qiuru, Sijing: Shen Zhiyao, Chen Qiusheng, Fengjing: Xu Beichen, He Jicai, Zhujing: Shen Zhonglian, Luxu: Yin Jingzhai, Wujiang: Jin Zhen'an, Suzhou: Chen Junyu, Tongli: Chen Songtao, Xu Yusheng, Pang Bosheng, Beita: Zhang Xiting, Zhang Guorong, Liantang: Zhu Xinhan, Shengze: Yang Lianqing, Cheng Yikuan, Pingwang: Lü Shaoyun, Gu Zhenzhong, Hengtang: Min Shaofu, Xitang: Min Yinqiao, Shen Chunlin, Pinghu: Zhang Pinghou, Cuanlai Temple: Zhuang Jieshen, Xindai: Lu Wenshan, Ji Weixian, Shanghai: Yan Xiaoquan, Zhu Zixiang, Shen Shangwen, Huang Shengyuan, Tong Fuhai, Zhu Qiu xiong, Li Shuiquan, Yang Yongyuan, Yan Jiyun, and 67 other representatives, along with more than 160 rice merchants. The meeting was called to order at 2 PM with a bell, chaired by Yan Xiaoquan, recorded by Wang Disheng, and conducted with proper formalities. The chairman reported on the approximate income and expenditure accounts for the twelfth year. Immediately following that, it was reported that letters had been received from the rice industry associations in Qingpu, Pinghu, Wujiang, Jiashan, Sijing, Jiaoli, and other ports, proposing matters concerning Shanghai rice firm commissions and pier donations. A letter had been forwarded to the Shanghai Bean and Rice Industry Association to question the logic, and the association's reply was read out. It was requested that the proposals be discussed. (1) Commission Case: The original commission was set at 20 cents per picul, and now it has increased by 2 cents. For us inland merchants, everything is included in the commission. Why is the Shanghai rice firm different? Therefore, the increased 2 cents should be deducted. The chairman then presented his opinion that the Shanghai rice firm commission, after being approved by the Social Affairs Bureau, is indeed only 20 cents. As for the increased 2 cents, the Bean and Rice Industry Association has explained clearly that it is the wage for porters and carriers, not for measures or wine. If you insist on deducting it, I am afraid that it will cause labor disputes. Please pay attention. After public discussion, it was decided to retain it. (2) Pier Donation Case: Pier donations are still being collected now, but the Bean and Rice Industry Association's account is not announced, so that payers know the details. It was resolved to send a letter to the Bean and Rice Industry Association, requesting that they promptly announce the account for the one cent pier fee paid before the end of June in detail, so that the northern city would be answered fully and donations would be stopped unanimously. (3) Sales Commission Case: The sales commission for rice in the northern city is 5 cents per picul, which the cargo owner is willing to pay. Qingpu traders must reduce the sales commission in southern Shanghai to the same treatment, and there should be no discrimination. It was resolved that the sales commission should be based on equality. Another meeting of merchants should be convened to reply to traders in various ports based on the circumstances. (4) A letter was received from various boatmen transporting rice, requesting leniency in the unloading order. It was resolved to reply to the boatmen and other parties to discuss with the cargo owner nearby, and the meeting adjourned. It was already 6 o'clock.

However, social customs often favor the purchase of foreign goods, so the promotion has yielded little results in half a year. Our capabilities are weak, and we are ashamed to say so. Recently, our association held a joint meeting of the Design, Economic, and Work Committees to discuss methods to continue promoting domestic goods for better implementation. It was unanimously agreed that domestic goods vendors and consumers must have a spirit of comprehensive cooperation in order to achieve practical results in promoting domestic goods. Household necessities are often filled with foreign goods, and it is difficult to identify the markings of domestic goods producers. As a result, once purchased, there is a risk of mistakenly purchasing inferior goods. It is requested that major companies uniformly label all kinds of domestic goods with the manufacturing factory and trademark, so that customers can easily identify them. In this atmosphere of enthusiastic promotion of domestic goods in the women's community, they will surely be happy to purchase domestic goods and avoid the drawbacks of mistakenly purchasing foreign goods. After discussion, it was decided to record the case and send a letter to your esteemed Chamber, requesting that you forward this instruction to all affiliated domestic goods companies, factories, and stores, and promptly implement it. Therefore, we send this letter with the resolution, hoping that you will investigate and handle it, as it is our sincere hope.

Letter from Ma Shaoquan, Executive Committee Member of the City Chamber of Commerce, to the Wuxi Fellow Association for Assistance to Wang Yingchun, the Bomb has been Rendered Harmless and Should Not Be Considered a Crime, and Young People with Potential Should Not Be Oppressed

Xin Sheng She states that Wang Yingchun, a young man from Wuxi and an employee of the New-New Company, was found to have a bomb during a dormitory search after a theft at the company. The police prosecuted him for endangering public safety under Article No. XXXX. Ma Shaoquan, the executive committee member of the City Chamber of Commerce and leader of the Wuxi community in Shanghai, sent a letter to the Wuxi Fellow Association out of fellow feeling, requesting assistance. The original letter reads: To the esteemed association, recently, I read in the evening newspaper that a young fellow villager, Wang Yingchun, was searched at the New-New Company after a theft and found to possess a bomb that had been rendered harmless and kept as a souvenir. The police are prosecuting him in the First Special District Court under Article No. XXXX, endangering public safety, etc. I have reviewed Wang's past. He is a young man with admirable ambition. The souvenir bomb has been rendered non-explosive. In all fairness, it should not be considered a crime. Furthermore, according to the police lawyer, Wang returned to the New-New Company after serving in the military and his conduct is good. Therefore, the law should be lenient. The New-New Company's search for stolen items and the discovery of the bomb are two completely separate matters. It seems inappropriate to destroy his potential and oppress him, depriving him of his freedom. Our association is a fellow villager. Young people with potential should be assisted. The bomb that has been rendered harmless should be quickly handed over to the police for safekeeping to prove its harmlessness. Therefore, I am sending this letter, hoping that you will investigate and handle it. Yours sincerely, to the Wuxi Fellow Association.

Rescuing Three Navigation Vessels

Italian Postal Ship Company, China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, Da Lai Company

Towing the Italian Ship

The Italian Postal Ship Company's freighter, the "Colt Le Treina", left Italy on the 15th of last month bound for Shanghai. Near Haiphong, Vietnam, it suddenly ran aground, delaying its arrival in Shanghai. It was reported in this newspaper. At the end of last month, it departed from Shanghai, first to various ports in Japan to load cargo, then to Hong Kong to return to Italy. On the 20th of this month, the ship was sailing about 100 nautical miles from Hong Kong, in the waters of Dongsha Island, when it ran aground on a shoal due to fog. The shipowner initially planned to sail out on his own, but because the hull was aground, he could not move. He telegraphed the Hong Kong and Shanghai companies for help. The Shanghai company received the report and telegraphed the freighter "Hihda" on its way to Shanghai to send goods. After leaving Singapore, it went directly to the location to tow the "Colt Le Treina" out of the shoal. It is expected that this will happen in the next day or two. The "Colt Le Treina" is purely a freighter and does not carry passengers and is not a regular scheduled ship, so the impact is light. However, the "Bult" was originally scheduled to arrive in Shanghai on the 29th, but this mission will require extending the date of arrival in Shanghai.

Jian Guo Escapes Danger

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Yangtze River ship, the "Jian Guo", was grounded in Tianjia Zhen on the 20th due to a broken rudder. The report stated before. The bureau later received a telegram from Jiujiang and a report from the "Jian Guo" shipowner, Wang Youshi, stating that after the "Jiang Shun" arrived, it used a wire cable to secure the "Jian Guo" and tried its best to tow it during the high tide. Fortunately, the Yangtze River was flooding, so once it was towed, it was pulled from the shoal. The cargo and passengers on the "Jian Guo" were spared the procedure of unloading and boarding the "Jiang Shun". However, because the rudder chain was broken and could not be steered, it was towed to Hankou by the "Wang Shun". The cargo is being unloaded and the rudder chain is being repaired. Today, it can be launched in Hankou and is scheduled to start operating in Shanghai on the 27th as usual.

Lincoln Goes to Hong Kong

The Dollar Steamship Line's "President Lincoln" caught fire in the Pacific, damaging the seventh cabin. Because it was a regular scheduled ship, it still arrived in Shanghai on the originally scheduled date. The burned and damaged goods in the seventh cabin have been unloaded at the White Lotus Wharf and are being inspected and counted. The ship manifest is being inspected every day and is very busy. Three cabins in the passenger area were damaged by water sprayed during firefighting and must also be repaired. Due to the time constraints, the ship departed from Shanghai at 2 PM yesterday and sailed to Hong Kong and the Philippines.

Southern District Rent Reduction Association Sends Letter to Property Owners Association Members, Hoping They Will Not Make Litigation a Means to an End

The Shanghai Southern District Rent Reduction Association held a meeting yesterday at the association's hall in Yongqingli, MinGuo Road, and resolved that, given the current situation of lawsuits filling the courts and disturbing society, the association solemnly declares that it will not participate in or hear any illegal actions of the spring bank if they do not act according to law to reduce rents. For those who have requested rent reductions to landlords, all rents must be deposited in the bank before a solution is reached and cannot be withdrawn at will. A request has also been submitted to the court. If there are any questions, please inquire at the association. The original letter to the Property Owners Association is recorded below. To the esteemed association, given the current economic situation and the decline of all of Shanghai, the call for rent reduction cannot be stopped. Please ask your members to consider the merchants' difficulties and, before the rent reduction negotiation is resolved, please ensure that those who have a bank deposit book with the association's seal proving that the rent has been deposited do not use rent arrears as an excuse to initiate lawsuits, so as to maintain feelings and support each other. If funds are needed, some can be withdrawn first, and then a solution can be sought. If lawsuits are initiated, the instigator will be fully responsible for the resulting losses. Please do not make litigation a means to an end and disturb society. We hope that you will carefully consider the advantages and disadvantages. We have long admired your association's ability to balance property and regulate finance, and we are confident that you can help the city's economy and seek a joint recovery. We hope that our humble suggestions will be adopted. Yours sincerely.

Pudong Electric Company Adds Submarine Cable; Jianghai Customs Issues Proclamation, Requiring All Shipping Companies to Pay Attention

The Pudong Electric Company and the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company connected to the power supply. In October of last year, a submarine cable was first laid across the river, from the east of Wuquan Road, North Jun Gong Road, Zhabei, to Pubin (approximately 1,130 meters from Nanqiujiang Port), to the company's distribution room in Taojiazha, Pudong. Now, for the safety of the power supply, another three-core submarine cable with a cross-sectional area of 125 square millimeters and a voltage of 6,600 volts has been ordered from the British Jardine Engineering Corporation. The cable is 850 meters long and is located downstream of the first cable, approximately 1,000 feet south of the Maluqiao gunpowder depot wharf, approximately 700 feet away. The laying was completed on the 5th of this month. Chinese warning signs "Cable Crossing Prohibit Anchoring" and English signs "Cable Crossing" are installed on both sides of the river and illuminated at night for identification. Proclamation No. 19 has been issued by the Jianghai Customs Harbour Master. The text is as follows: Jianghai Customs Harbour Master's Proclamation No. 19 for the installation of a new power cable in the new waterway. It is hereby announced that a new power cable has been installed approximately 700 feet south of the Maluqiao gunpowder depot wharf, crossing the new waterway, approximately 1,000 feet downstream of the first power cable. On the shore at both ends of the cable, there are advertising signs and lights are lit in front of the signs at night to identify them. All shipping companies are hereby notified to pay attention. June 20, 23rd Year of the Republic of China, signed Harbour Master You Lien, Deputy Harbour Master Luo Man Luo.

China Merchants Bureau's Resident Supervisor in England Telegraphed that Seagoing Ships Will be Completed, 70-80% of the Project Has Been Completed, and After Arriving in Shanghai, They Will Definitely Sail on the South China Route

The state-run China Merchants Bureau borrowed funds from the British Boxer Indemnity Fund to build four seagoing ships in England, which have been named Haiyuan, Haiheng, Haili, and Haizhen. Wu Daming and others have been sent to England for supervision. The Shanghai General Bureau has now received a telegram from the supervisor stating that 85% or 70% of the construction of the four seagoing ships has been completed. They will be completed and sail to China one after another from the end of October to the end of this year. It is reported that General Manager Liu Hongsheng has decided that after the seagoing ships arrive in Shanghai, they will sail on the South China route, and the original South China route ships will be transferred to the Northern route. As for opening up the Southeast Asia route, it will be decided based on the business situation when the seagoing ships arrive in Shanghai.

The organization of the theater has created an unprecedented record in the Shanghai ticket industry, so it is known as the civil and military theater. Huasheng Factory Offers Prizes for Predicting the Heat of the Summer This Year; Those Who Guess Correctly Will Receive Electric Fans

Huasheng Electric Appliance Manufacturing Factory, in order to stimulate the interest of all sectors and test psychology, is holding a summer heat prediction event. All those who guess correctly will be given electric fans as souvenirs. The prediction method and distribution of prizes are listed below. A. Prediction method: (1) Specify the highest temperature at 12:00 noon on one day from July 10th to July 31st as the qualifying temperature. (2) The highest temperature must be specified to the nearest degree and tenth of a degree, using Fahrenheit as the standard. (3) Applicants must fill out the prediction form (see separate form), cut out the Huasheng trademark, paste it in the corner, and mail it. (4) The highest temperature is based on the Shanghai Observatory report as the standard temperature. (5) The deadline for prediction letters is July 9th. (6) The above predictions will be announced in the newspaper before August 15th based on the Shanghai Observatory report. B. Distribution of prizes: (1) Those who predict the same as the standard temperature will be given a 56-inch ceiling fan, worth 78 yuan. (2) Those who predict the standard temperature off by 1.0 degrees will be given a 16-inch table fan, worth 40 yuan. (3) Those who predict the standard temperature off by only 1.0 degree. (4) The above prizes are limited to one per person, in order of when the prediction form is received.

Hu Yuanxiang, a Ningbo native and manager of Jingda Xiang Hardware Store, testified that he and Zhu Lianyou were friends. When Wang was an apprentice at Ruixingshun, he was a colleague in that store for six or seven years. That day, Wang had been to his store. He knew that Wang had always been well-behaved. The judge then ordered the fourth defendant, Tang Qingyue, to be brought to the stand and said that he only knew Zhang Zuming, but was not a friend. Four or five years ago, he called him to see a doctor. He had no feud with Zhang. After he was arrested this time, he confronted Zhang in the police station. Zhang said he was not there, and he himself

Also Did Not Admit

he was there. On the fifth of this month, he saw seven outpatients at Dade Hospital in the afternoon, and they are all here and can testify, and presented a clinic log as evidence. Then the patient's family members Zhang Jiu, Chen Zhou, Yin Fang, three students from the Dade Midwifery School, Jin Meiyun, Wang Wuirui, and Hu Kejing, three people testified that Tang Qingyue was indeed working in the hospital school that afternoon and had not left, etc. At this point, the time had passed five o'clock. The judge ordered each witness to

Sign an Affidavit

and file it. He announced that the case would be adjourned to the 28th of this month for further trial. Zhang, Zhuang, and Wang were remanded in custody, and Tang was released on his original bail and informed the defendants' lawyers that if they had any evidence to present, they could submit a written statement to the court for further investigation. The lawyers for Zhang, Zhuang, and Wang all said that the case had been investigated by the police, and the defendants had been wrongly detained for a long time, and requested that they be allowed to post joint bail and be released to await trial and that there was no danger of escape. If the police needed to summon them for questioning, the defense lawyers could be notified by telephone and they could immediately appear in court, etc. The court did not pronounce judgment on the case and changed the date for a very short time, and temporarily suspended bail, so the court adjourned.

Monument to Fallen Police Officers Scheduled for Unveiling Ceremony; Director Wen Invites All Circles to Attend

The Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau, in order to commend the police officers who have died in the line of duty in the past, and to provide an example for future generations to admire, has specially built a stone monument at the intersection of Baoshan Road and Hongxing Road in Zhabei to commemorate them forever. The entire project has been completed and will be unveiled at 10:00 AM on the 26th of this month. Director Wen Hongen yesterday sent invitations to various agencies and organizations in the city, inviting them to send representatives to attend the ceremony at that time. The details are as follows:

Appearance of the Monument

The Monument to Fallen Police Officers of Past Years is located at the intersection of Baoshan Road and Hongxing Road in Zhabei and was designed by architect Fan Wenzhao. It covers an area of about a quarter of an acre and is triangular in shape. A stone monument is built in the center, with a height of more than two zhang. From the base to the top, it is all made of white stone. The center of the monument is engraved with "Monument to Fallen Police Officers of Shanghai in Past Years." The lower end is the inscription of the monument. Both sides and the back are the names of the fallen police officers of past years. The road around the monument is paved with cement. As of March 1934, there were a total of 235 fallen police officers.

Invitation to All Circles to Attend

The Municipal Public Security Bureau issued an invitation yesterday, saying: "This is to inform you that the unveiling ceremony of the Monument to Fallen Police Officers of Past Years will be held at 10:00 AM on June 26th of the Gregorian calendar. You are respectfully invited to attend and provide guidance. Ordered by Wen Hongen, Director of the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau."

Scenes of Inland China Captured by Foreign Cameras; Mr. Meisai of America Talks with Western Newspaper Reporter

The "North China Daily News" reports that Mr. Meisai of Metro-Goldwyn-Mayer Pictures, of America, has made a film based on the novel "The Good Earth" by American female writer Pearl Buck, and has taken local scenes in inland China. He has spent five months here and yesterday (22nd) took a boat back to America. Afterwards he plans to complete the film. He told the "North China Daily News" reporter that he was very grateful for the various assistance given by the Nanjing government and the Nanjing Film Censorship Bureau. His work is indeed pioneering. Taking location shots in China by a foreign film company is unprecedented. He believes that once the mountains and forests are opened, other foreign companies will follow suit. He is sure that his company will make new films in China in the near future. He had photographed all the way from Shanghai to Beiping and as far as Shanhaiguan. It was supposed to take seven weeks to complete the work, but it has been extended to five months. The company had sent 15 artists to travel with him and hired personnel as needed in various locations. The cost of the film far exceeded expectations, but the cost was well worth it. After arriving in the United States, it will take five or six months to complete the entire film. All the films taken were produced in Shanghai and shown to the Nanjing Film Censorship Bureau before going to the United States. Very few were deleted.

Mr. Mei also told a reporter from the "Continental Daily News" that there was a representative of the Nanjing government at the scene when filming along the way. In the future, when making interior scenes in Hollywood, there will also be a representative of the Nanjing government. After the entire film is completed, it will be sent to Nanjing for approval. Most of the films taken have not yet been made, and those that have been made are very satisfactory after being shown.

Various Circles in Pudong Hold a Lantern Parade to Promote the New Life Movement

Various circles in Pudong held a lantern parade at 7:00 PM last night to implement the New Life Movement. It was jointly initiated by the Party, police, security, and various public organizations and schools. After several meetings, officials were appointed to carry out preparations separately, and participating lantern groups were notified to gather on Pudong Avenue before 7:00 PM last night and depart on time. Participants in the parade included members of the Five District Party Headquarters and various branch party members, police officers from the Third District Public Security Bureau and various branch stations, members of the security guard group headquarters and various sub-teams, students from municipal private primary and secondary schools, and personnel from various agricultural, industrial, and commercial public organizations, totaling more than 1,000 people. The various lanterns made all conformed to the purpose of the New Life Movement and also promoted the spirit of martial arts, making various new military equipment in order to awaken the public. The parade proceeded north along Pudong Avenue, directly to Lujiazai, turned into Beihutang Road, went south along Laiyidu Street, passed Lujia Ferry, reached Yangjia Ferry, turned east to Zhenxiu [street name missing], passed Shenjia Alley, and returned to Pudong Avenue to disband. The lanterns were brilliant along the way, and the drums and music were loud. The streets were packed with spectators, which was a unprecedented event in Pudong. Various agencies, organizations, and schools also hung flags and tied colored streamers yesterday, and various shops also hung lanterns, which were beautiful and dazzling. The atmosphere on the roads was completely new.

National Exhibition Announces Business Numbers for Three Weeks; During the Exhibition Period, There Will Be Rotating Price Cuts and Sacrifices; A Banquet Will Be Held Regularly to Entertain Reporters and Distribute Gifts

The National Products Movement Exhibition at the Penglai Market in Shanghai was originally scheduled to last for two weeks, from the 1st to the 21st of this month. Because the exhibition has been very successful and various factories participating in the exhibition have requested an extension of the closing date, the association convened a general meeting of all factory representatives on the 20th and unanimously resolved to extend the exhibition by nine days, until the 30th of this month. During the extended exhibition period, all participating factories will re-arrange their displays, and the temporary business area will have daily price cuts. The association has released the business statistics and the number of visitors for the past three weeks.

Three-Week Statistics

According to statistics released by the association's statistics department, the business volume of the temporary business area and the number of visitors for the past three weeks are as follows: In the first week, the number of visitors was more than 258,000 and the business volume was more than 148,300 yuan. In the second week, the number of visitors was more than 283,000 and the business volume was more than 172,000 yuan. In the third week, the number of visitors was more than 214,000 and the business volume was more than 110,800 yuan. The total number of visitors for the three weeks was more than 760,000, and the total business volume was more than 432,000 yuan.

Re-arrangement

After the association decided to extend the closing date by nine days, the venue was re-arranged and thousands of colorful electric torches were added. Factories such as Limin Dyeing and Weaving Factory, Yansheng Industrial Society, Fuxin Cloth Factory, Meiya Silk Factory, Dachina Rubber Factory, Yaubuer Electric Appliance Factory, Minsheng Rubber Factory, Shanghai Enamel Factory, and Guangdong Brothers Rubber Factory all scheduled to reduce prices, and redecorated the interior to have a new look, making people feel overwhelmed.

Scheduled Banquet

All the factories of the association believe that the exhibition has received enthusiastic support and widespread publicity from the public opinion, so the results of this exhibition are better than before. Therefore, most factories initiated a plan to invite the Shanghai press to a banquet on the 29th of this month and distribute national product gifts to express their enthusiasm.

Lawyer Cao Lin is accused of inducing Wang Meiying, a woman under the age of 20, into illicit relations, and after she became pregnant, abandoning her. In June of last year, Meiying, because it was a Sunday and it was very hot, went to the

Zhaofeng Garden

to cool off at 4:00 or 5:00 PM, when the sun was setting. The child fell to the ground while playing in the circle. Their Relationship Grew Closer

chat. Unexpectedly, Cao suddenly closed the door tightly and demanded to sleep with her. Meiying, believing she was still a virgin, did not want to defile herself and firmly refused. Dance School

簡照南妾 訴養女案訊結 定二十七日宣判

The case of Jian Liang Jingfen, the concubine of the deceased Jian Zhaonan, shareholder of Nanyang Brothers Tobacco Company, suing her adopted daughter Jian Zhenyi, who left without saying goodbye on March 11th of this year, and repeatedly refused to return, considering the relationship severed, immediately hired a lawyer to file a petition with the Civil Court of the First Special Court requesting adoption termination. The court, considering Jian Zhenyi's minority status, legally appointed lawyer Jiang Yiping as a special agent. After three summons by the court, Jian Zhenyi argued that the reason for leaving was that Jian Liang had an affair with the venerable Ben Ji of Baohua Mountain. Recently, Ben Ji repeatedly attempted to violate her chastity and committed various unspeakable acts against her, forcing her to leave. She also filed a counterclaim, demanding that Jian Liang pay education, upbringing, and marriage expenses of 30,000 yuan each. This was reported in this newspaper. Yesterday afternoon, Peng Shi of the court continued the hearing. Lawyer Jiang Yiping was unable to attend due to other commitments and delegated lawyer Wu Baotai as his representative. Lawyer Wu stated that a settlement was absolutely impossible. The court then ordered the commencement of arguments. Lawyer He, representing the plaintiff, stated that the defendant, after being raised and educated by the plaintiff for eighteen years, left without saying goodbye and made various insults to the plaintiff. Therefore, in accordance with Articles 1081 and 1086 of the Civil Code, he requested a judgment terminating the adoption. Furthermore, the defendant's claim that her upbringing expenses were included in the 60,000 yuan received by the plaintiff was completely wrong. This 60,000 yuan was a one-time living expense paid by Pan, the legal wife of Jian Zhaonan. Therefore, he requested that her suit be dismissed. Lawyer Wu argued that the reason for the defendant's departure had been explained, and the defendant's suffering should be understood. The plaintiff claimed that she had repeatedly tried to get the defendant back, but in reality, she could not return. The defendant had previously stated that she could return home as long as Ben Ji did not come, but the plaintiff could not accept this condition. How could she favor a monk over her adopted daughter? Therefore, he requested that the plaintiff's suit be dismissed and that if the adoption was terminated, the defendant's economic situation would be in dire straits. According to Article 1082 of the Civil Code, she should be given a considerable sum of money. Furthermore, the defendant had a right to the 60,000 yuan, and he requested a judgment for 30,000 yuan. The court then ordered the conclusion of the arguments and set the judgment date for the 27th.

蘇州河沿岸 住船貧民起鬨 擊沉代表船屋三艘 認警局佈告係僞造

Along the Suzhou River, from Chadaijiao in the west to the New Garbage Bridge in the east, bordered by the Public Concession to the south and Zhabei Chinese area to the north, since last spring, the Dredging Bureau believed that the boat dwellings of the poor on both sides of the river hindered their work. Therefore, they petitioned the Municipal Government to find a way to expel them. Later, the Municipal Government, considering that these poor people were ignorant and unreasonable, allowed them to continue living there. However, the elements among these poor people were complex, and a radical solution had to be used. Only the original residents were allowed to decrease, and no new residents were allowed to increase. Seven measures were established, and representatives Jiang Weiqing, Zhou Bokai, Li Ruizhen, Shang Longyou, Tang Cunjie, Jiang Deyu, Zhao Ruyi, Li Guifu, Li Youfa, Ni Jingui, Liang Rengui, Zhou Chongshan, and Sun Yougui were selected from among these poor people to be responsible for investigation and registration. Unexpectedly, this had not been implemented until this year. The Municipal Government then ordered the Public Security Bureau to instruct Xu Chizhi, Inspector of the Second Water Patrol Team, to carry out the registration and issued a notice. This caused a major uproar. For some unknown reason, these poor people, around 10 p.m. the night before, gathered a crowd of five to six hundred men, women, old, and young, and rushed to the boat dwellings of the representatives, hitting anyone they encountered without asking why. The representatives, seeing the unfavorable situation, led their families to escape. As a result, one boat dwelling each of Shang Longyou at the entrance of Xingyi Lane on Guangfu Road, Shen Jiazhong at the entrance of Yuanshun Timber Company, were sunk and completely destroyed. The boats of Chen Jinsheng and Cheng Haiquan were also damaged. The boat dwelling of Li Ruizhen on the riverbank of Yong'an Cotton Mill in the concession area was also completely destroyed. It is now known that these representatives have submitted petitions to the Municipal Government and the Public Security Bureau, seeking relief. According to these poor people, the representatives forged a notice from the Public Security Bureau to sow discord, so they had to put the representatives to death. Their ignorance is both ridiculous and pitiful.

徐家宅路 盜匪越貨殺人 蔡李氏盛裝賈禍 呼救中槍竟枉死

At No. 58 Xujiazhai Road, Zhabei, Jiangbei native Cai Yutian and his wife Cai Li lived in a thatched hut. The couple was able to be diligent and thrifty, so they had some savings. However, the woman dressed in elaborate clothing to flaunt her wealth. Around 8 p.m. the night before, Cai was already asleep when the woman, wearing gold bracelets and rings, went out to soak her feet. On her way home, three robbers, seeing her wealth, were tempted and followed her home. When the woman returned home, the robbers also entered and robbed her by force. When the woman shouted for help, the robbers opened fire, shooting her once in the left breast, causing her to fall to the ground immediately. They robbed her of two gold rings and fled. Cai, hearing the noise in the room, rushed out and saw that his wife had been shot and killed. He mourned loudly over her body and reported the incident to the Fourth District Police Station, which sent police to investigate but without success. Yesterday, the local bailiff, Lu Abaobao, was ordered to report the case to the local court. Prosecutor Wu and others were commissioned to the scene to examine the body and confirmed that she died from a gunshot wound. They ordered the family to collect the body and wait for the arrest of the murderer and investigation of the case.

來函

To the Editor, After reading the article in your newspaper on the 18th of this month about the large-scale shipment of Japanese straw hats to Shanghai for dumping, I was shocked. It is found that there are about seventy or eighty straw hat manufacturers in Shanghai, both large and small. The larger ones include Huafu, Huanqiu, Huaxing, FulI, Guanyi, Fuyuan, Huang Shaoji, Cao Chengji, and Dong Huasheng, among others, all of which are members of our association. They completely use domestic raw materials to manufacture straw hats and promote them throughout the country. As for Japanese straw hats, they have almost completely disappeared in recent years. Our colleagues have not promoted them on their behalf. As for the annual output of more than 50,000 dozen, it is also inconsistent with the original number of manufacturers. Among them, Shanghai, Zhonghua, and Yongli are not members of our association, so we cannot prove it for them. At this time of advocating domestic goods, I am afraid that the people of the country do not understand the truth, which hinders the sales of domestic goods. For this reason, I am sending this letter to your newspaper, please publish it in the letter column so that the people of the country can understand. This is to the person in charge of Shen Bao, the Shanghai Straw and Felt Hat Industry Association, June 23.
