Reading Q&A

動物有沒有本能？（一）

Do animals have instincts? (1)

丨丨 Reply to Mr. Wang Deming

After reading Guo Renyuan's "Common Basis of Behavioral Science", Mr. Wang had great doubts about the behaviorists' denial of "instinct" and "consciousness". Mr. Wang believes that "people have instincts" and at the same time Mr. Wang also "respects instinct theory." Who is right and who is wrong? Mr. Wang himself cannot decide, so he asks us. We feel that the question raised, although it is inevitably too specialized, but the theory of "instinct" has a deep impression on the general public, and we believe that it is not meaningless to take this opportunity to discuss it once! Before explaining human "instincts", we should discuss animal instincts, so we have slightly expanded the question. Now let's briefly discuss methodology.

It is generally accepted by psychologists that animals have instincts, but behavioral psychologists uniquely object to it, especially Mr. Guo Renyuan is the most thorough. Will instinct really lose its meaning of existence due to the opposition of behaviorists? This is a very worthy question to discuss. But if you want to get a satisfactory solution from the research and theories of various schools of psychology today, it is very difficult, because each school has its own source of standpoint and method, and each school adheres to its own right and opposes others' wrongs. The conclusions reached are often one-sided.

We naturally cannot deny that each school of psychologists has made its special contributions to psychology, but at the same time, their one-sided, metaphysical methodology prevents them from grasping the overall situation of things, leading the conclusions to extremely dangerous aspects. Behaviorism has also provided many valuable studies, and at the same time, because of the special methods of behaviorism, it has reached very strange conclusions, namely the denial of instinct.

Therefore, to answer the question of whether there are instincts after all, it is best to first make a critique of the methods of behaviorism and point out what is the correct research method. Grasping the correct method, readers can make correct judgments in the research, and will not be at a loss when they see a strange conclusion.

The value of behaviorism lies in the fact that it applies materialistic, thorough experimental methods in psychology. In the hands of behaviorists, psychology has become a completely objective experimental science. It also regards psychological phenomena as a kind of material phenomenon, and as a process of a series of stimuli and responses. Therefore, behaviorists believe that the research of psychological science should be to apply material stimuli to seek the material response behavior on animals. The research of stimuli and responses is the fundamental basis of psychological science. Behaviorists abandoned the subjective observation method of introspectionists and treated the mind as the same thing as physics and chemistry.

Linking psychological phenomena with physics and chemistry is a great achievement of behaviorism, because higher-level (psychological) phenomena cannot be separated from lower-level material foundations. Psychological action is only an attribute of material action. When matter does not exist, there is no mind. Obtaining an understanding of the mind from the study of matter is a great advantage of behaviorism. However, once behaviorism grasps the material foundation, it thinks that this low-level foundation is already sufficient to represent everything, so it denies the particularity of the entire psychological action, thinking that there is nothing more than the process of stimulation and response. Instinct, consciousness, can be reduced to the phenomenon of stimulation and response, and it itself has no meaning at all.

Based on this methodology, behaviorists deny the existence of instinct and regard instinct as one of the processes of stimulation and response. This methodology is what we often hear called "mechanistic methodology." Reducing higher-level phenomena to lower-level phenomena and obliterating the special significance of higher-level phenomena. More clearly, mechanists believe that higher-level phenomena and lower-level phenomena only have differences in complexity and simplicity, but no difference in nature, that is, only quantitative differences, but no qualitative differences. Therefore, it is believed that instinct and the process of stimulation and response are the same thing, but stimulation and response are only simple stimulation and response, and instinct is only a series of complex stimulations and responses.

This methodology is also metaphysical. Why is it metaphysical? It is that it grasps one side of things and forgets the other side of things. It regards the side it grasps as dead and fixed, and does not know the activity of this side, does not know that it can be transformed into the other side. Acknowledging the low-level phenomena of stimulation and response, and abandoning the high-level phenomena such as instinct and consciousness, this is metaphysics.

But the metaphysical method has long ceased to be a method of studying truth today. To give a simple example, water is more advanced than hydrogen and oxygen, because water is a compound formed by the combination of hydrogen and oxygen, but can we say that the properties of water are the same as those of hydrogen and oxygen? Naturally, to study the composition of water, it must be decomposed into these two gases, but the understanding of the nature of water itself can never be obtained in the study of the two gases, but the whole water must be taken for research. We cannot deny the special nature of advanced water because we analyze out low-level hydrogen and oxygen. When low-level phenomena are compounded into high-level phenomena, it is not only a quantitative change, that is, not only a quantitative complexity, but also a change in nature, and it is transformed into another kind of quality.

Therefore, studying high-level phenomena with the analysis of low-level phenomena as the foundation is something that can be agreed with, because high-level phenomena are composed of low-level phenomena, and high-level phenomena contain all low-level phenomena. But once a high-level phenomenon is formed, the properties of the low-level phenomenon disappear and become another kind of property. This process of transformation is what is called sublation (Aufheben). In this way, for behaviorists, we can greatly admire their materialistic, objective, experimental research methods, but because of the application of this method, we must deny the instinct and consciousness of animals. That is the work of the metaphysical method. If we break the shackles of the metaphysical viewpoint, we can admit the existence of instinct, at least there is no need to deny it. Because instinct is a more advanced phenomenon than simple stimulation and response, although it is also composed of a series of stimuli and responses, but since it has become a series, the nature is not just a stimulation response. For example, a simple stimulus response is only a mechanical, blind behavior, while instinct is a purposeful behavior that stubbornly moves around a central purpose. Since instinct's purposeful behavior is different from mechanical blind behavior, the special meaning of instinct can be established, and the existence of instinct cannot be denied. (To be continued)

Mixed Doubles Semifinals: Qiu Feihai's Team Eliminated, Loses to Ke Erqiao's Team 1-2

The mixed doubles competition of the Shanghai Lawn Tennis Club was held yesterday at the French Chamber of Commerce, with Qiu Feihai and Madame Medemo facing Ke Erqiao and Madame Tui Lou in the semifinals. As a result, the Qiu-Mei team lost 1-2 and was eliminated. The Ke-La Sha siblings against Bu De and Mrs. Ni Gushi will be held today.

Ke Erqiao & Mrs. Tui Lou beat Qiu Feihai & Madame Medemo four to six, six to four, six to one.

Technical Decline

Qiu Feihai's technique is noticeably declining. His shots are soft and lack power, and his net play cannot overcome the opponent's desperate situations. Madame Medemo was initially good and coped with ease, but later she became completely useless, hitting the net with every shot. It was quite difficult for the two to win the first set, as Qiu's performance was affected by Madame Medemo's poor showing.

Excellent Net Play

The opponent, Madame Tui Lou, is slender, in stark contrast to the large Madame Medemo. Their techniques are similar, but Madame Tui Lou can persevere consistently. Ke Erqiao, though not a top player, has dangerous net play, always watching intently. All incoming balls are intercepted, preventing Qiu Feihai from displaying his strengths.

Match Summary

The first and second sets were fiercely contested, with each game tied several times, making it difficult to determine the winner. In the first set, Qiu initially lost 2-3 and 3-4, but eventually won 6-4. In the second set, the Qiu team initially won two games but then lost five consecutive games. They tried hard to rally, catching up to 4-5. In the next game, it rained heavily, and the game was played in the rain, resulting in Qiu's loss and the loss of the set. The rain stopped after that. In the third set, the Qiu team was at a loss, and the opponents won easily with a score of 6-1.

National Sports Association to Build Three Tennis Courts

▲One Hard Court, Two Grass Courts

▲Basketball Court Also in the Plans

Since moving the grounds a few days ago, the China National Sports Advancement Association has been greatly expanding its internal facilities, as previously reported. It is now known that only a portion has not yet been moved. It has been decided to build three tennis courts, one hard court and two grass courts. The courts will be located north of the soccer field, and construction is being overseen by Ke Zheng, with completion expected by the end of this month. The grass needed for the grass tennis courts will be supplied from the existing grass on the baseball field. The construction of a basketball court is currently being planned, and if finances are not an issue, construction can begin within this year. The location has been tentatively set north of the soccer field and west of the tennis courts. Due to the terrain and contractual relationships, the track and field and baseball fields will be combined with the soccer field. In addition, the Association, due to the lack of tap water in Shen Yuan, is currently overseeing the digging of a well to supply water.

This City Organizes Youth Holiday Service Corps

▲The Municipal Education Bureau Convened a Meeting of Principals of Secondary Schools and Above Yesterday

▲The Corps Leader is Director Pan, and the Deputy Corps Leaders are the Principals of Various Schools

In order to organize the city's Youth Holiday Service Corps, the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau convened a meeting of principals of secondary schools and above in the city at the Shanghai YMCA at 2:00 PM yesterday. Principals from over 70 schools attended the meeting, and it was decided on the spot that each school would organize a sub-corps and determine the minimum number of groups. Details are as follows:

Participating Schools

Yesterday, principals from over 70 schools, including Daxia, Lida, Guangxia, Pudong, Minli, Zhonghua Vocational School, Private Shanghai Middle School, Municipal North, Zhengshi Minzhi, Fudan, Yangjing, Aiguo, Huadong, Shanghai Women's Middle School, Minli Women's Middle School, Jingye Xinlu, Zhirenyong, Jianguo, Chengzhong Yucai, Xuhui, Qingnian, Junyi, Nanyang, Kunfan, Nanyang Model, Datong Wusong, Jiangxi Vocational School, Guangzhao, etc., attended.

Director's Report

First, Director Pan reported that the purpose of convening the meeting of principals of secondary schools and above in the city today was to organize the Youth Holiday Service Corps. Half a month ago, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek sent a telegram to the education departments and bureaus of various provinces and cities, hoping that students above the middle school level could use their holidays to do social service work. The Jiangxi Education Department has taken the lead in formulating measures and will implement them starting this summer vacation. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek instructed the Jiangxi Education Department to provide the measures to various provinces and cities for reference and instructed the education departments and bureaus of various regions to convene meetings of principals of middle schools and above to discuss the measures. This city, together with the Jiangsu Education Department, formulated a set of measures that are slightly different from those of Jiangxi due to different local environments. This year is the first time for experimentation, and it is hoped that preparations will be better before the winter vacation than for the summer vacation, he said.

Points to Note

Director Pan then explained the organizational measures and service details, with the following points to note: (1) The Youth Holiday Service Corps is organized by students in secondary schools and above, but elementary school teachers and staff who wish to participate may also do so. (2) It is hoped that principals of various schools will actively promote this at the beginning of implementation to encourage students to participate. Each school should organize a sub-corps, and the principals of each school will serve as deputy corps leaders. The Education Bureau will distribute appointment letters within one or two days. (3) Each school may consider the situation and arrange the students' work steps. A guiding outline should be prepared in advance. (4) Each sub-corps should be divided into groups, and the operation methods of the groups can be determined by each school. Regardless of whether the group or individual is the unit, the scope of work must be determined. (5) Each school must treat this work as extracurricular work for students and stipulate assessment measures to assess their performance. (6) All application forms, guiding outlines, assessment measures, etc., should be prepared in duplicate, one copy stored in the sub-corps and one copy sent to the Education Bureau by the end of June.

Organizational Measures

(1) The purpose of this corps is to use the holidays to promote youth group training and cultivate the spirit of serving society. (2) The scope of service of this corps is to promote the New Life Movement as the main task and popularize literacy as the secondary task. (3) All teachers and staff and students of the school who wish to join this corps and have been approved by the principal may become basic members. People from all walks of life who wish to join this corps and have been introduced by one basic member may become members. All must fill out an application form. (4) This corps shall have one corps leader, concurrently held by the director of the Education Bureau, and several deputy corps leaders, concurrently held by the principals of various schools, to assist the corps leader in handling all matters. (5) The service of this corps is divided into three groups: special zone, city, and rural. Each deputy corps leader shall have one chief director to be appointed by teachers and staff to handle all matters of the group under the direction of the deputy corps leader. (6) Each special zone group, city group, and rural group shall have several subgroups, organized by three to five members, with one subgroup leader. (7) This corps may establish a guidance committee when necessary, and its organizational measures shall be formulated separately. (Service details of this corps shall be formulated separately.)

Service Details

(1) These details are formulated in accordance with Article 8 of the Organizational Measures of the Shanghai Municipal Youth Holiday Service Corps. (2) The scope of service of this corps is as follows: (A) Special Zone Group: (1) Promote attention to courtesy; (2) Promote compliance with public reason; (3) Promote domestic goods; (4) Promote sports; (5) Promote unity and cooperation; (6) Advocate thrift; (7) Promote cleanliness and hygiene; (8) Establish amateur tutorial schools; (9) Popularize literacy movement; (10) Other matters to improve customs. (B) City Group: (1) Promote attention to courtesy; (2) Promote compliance with public reason; (3) Promote domestic goods; (4) Instill patriotic concepts; (5) Promote sports; (6) Advocate thrift; (7) Promote cleanliness and hygiene; (8) Establish amateur tutorial schools; (9) Popularize literacy movement; (10) Other matters to improve customs. (C) Rural Group: (1) Promote attention to courtesy; (2) Promote compliance with discipline; (3) Instill patriotic concepts; (4) Promote sports and beneficial physical and mental entertainment; (5) Discourage smoking, drinking, gambling, and welcoming gods and temple fairs; (6) Lead farmers and workers to study production knowledge; (7) Hold literacy campaigns to effectively teach illiterate people to read; (9) Other matters beneficial to rural areas. (3) This corps should make full use of the following holidays for service: (1) Summer vacation; (2) Winter vacation; (3) Spring vacation; (4) Sundays; (5) Other holidays. (4) Each subgroup should select work items according to the environment of their hometown and formulate work steps and methods before the holiday, under the direction of the deputy corps leader and group director, and implement them accordingly. (5) Each subgroup should have a kind and sincere attitude in their service, use persuasion and edification methods, and seek the belief of the public so that they can happily accept and follow them. (6) The working methods of each subgroup can be determined according to the nature of the identified work, whether it is a meeting lecture, separate persuasion, liaison with local gentry to discuss progress, or participation in existing social organizations to assist in improvement. (7) The working location of each subgroup may be negotiated and used, such as mountains, forests, beaches, open-air fields, docks, temples, guild halls, and other public places, or temporary sheds may be built, or families may be persuaded separately. (8) If there are more than two subgroups in one place, they should be effectively linked to increase work efficiency. (9) When each subgroup returns to school after the holiday, they should report their work achievements to the group director in writing and forward them to the deputy corps leader. (10) The deputy corps leader and the group director should guide and assess the holiday service of each subgroup, encourage them, and report to the corps leader. (10) (2) The service of this corps is a training for young people to serve the community and is undertaken voluntarily. If a small amount of funding is needed for the work, it should be raised by each subgroup. (10) (2) These details may be amended at any time if there are any matters not covered.

The Municipal Education Bureau, Upon the Order of the Ministry, Will Hold a Summer Training Class for Middle School Science Teachers

▲Designated to be Co-organized with Jiaotong and Datong Universities

▲Location at Jiaotong, Starting July 16

The Municipal Education Bureau, upon the order of the Ministry, will hold a summer training class for science teachers in middle schools in Shanghai, co-organized with National Jiaotong University and Private Datong University, to provide incumbent science teachers in various middle schools in the city with opportunities for further study during the summer vacation. The bureau and the two universities have assigned Chen Bai, Xie En'gao, Zhang Yongchun, Zhang Xifang, Xu Guiquan, Qiu Weiyu, Xu Mingcai, Hu Dunfu, and other eight people to jointly organize a preparatory committee, which has convened two meetings and decided that the location will be at Jiaotong University. The training subjects will be divided into four groups: mathematics, physics, chemistry, and biology. The duration will be from July 16th to August 15th. Registration will be handled one week before the deadline. Classes will be held for two hours in the morning and discussions and experiments will be held for two hours each in the afternoon, held on alternate days. Each member will be required to pay more than ten yuan for tuition, accommodation, experiment fees, and lecture notes, which will be borne by the original school. It is reported that the committee is actively drafting the regulations so that each school can register students to attend the class.

Report on the Start of the Children's Health Camp

The Shanghai Summer Children's Health Camp is jointly organized by the Health and Education Bureaus, the Morning Post, the Anti-Tuberculosis Association, and the Children's Happiness Association. Its content focuses on children's physical health and strength. Therefore, doctors and psychologists are hired to guide matters related to diet and nutrition, medical examinations, sleep and rest, games and sports, hygiene habits, and bathing cleanliness, so that children become stronger after entering the camp. From today onwards, enrollment will be conducted at three locations: the Morning Post, the Chinese Tuberculosis Prevention Association, and the Municipal South Clinic, for a period of six weeks. Only a food fee of thirteen yuan and a tonic fee of three yuan are charged. Because the daily meals are prepared by nutrition experts, such as milk, chicken, vegetables, fruits, and cod liver oil, are all properly allocated, each person needs to pay about ten yuan. The camp has prepared more than a thousand yuan for running the camp. It is reported that there are many applicants, and if it exceeds one hundred people, additional personnel will be hired and the environment will be expanded to accommodate them.

The Central University in the Past Two Years (Continued)

— Luo Jialun

(B) Library and Instrument Equipment. School equipment, apart from academic buildings, mainly consists of library and instrument equipment. The current policy is to strive to save administrative expenses to expand the former equipment. Therefore, it is a source of academic teaching and research and cannot be ignored for a moment. Looking back, although the allocation for this equipment was high, there was a year in which the actual expenditure for library and instrument equipment was only 36,582 yuan. In these twenty-one months (up to May 31 of this year), the library fee paid was 142,461 yuan. There are still more than 20,000 yuan that have been determined but not yet paid, which have not been included. A total of 27,458 new Chinese books, 12,138 Western books, 602 Chinese magazines, and 571 Western magazines have been added. The number of copies can be estimated on a regular basis. In particular, supplementing the missing Western magazines in the 20th year of the Republic of China makes people feel the difficulty of the burden. However, the most gratifying thing is that in this short period, all 24 Western magazines have been purchased, such as "Journal furdie reineund angewandteMathematik" from 1826 to the present, a total of 109 years, "MathematischeAnnalen" from 1869 to the present, a total of 65 years, "Berichte der DeuIschen Bctaniechen Gesellschaft" from 1883 to the present, a total of 51 years, "Harvard Iaw Rcvie w" from 1887 to the present, a total of 47 years, have all been purchased. Among them, the most expensive one costs six to seven thousand yuan a set, but for the sake of research, no expense is spared to purchase it.

As for the instrument equipment, the actual expenditure in these twenty-one months was 246,819 yuan and four cents, not counting those that have been determined but not yet arrived. Those listed under consumables have not been totaled, and there are thousands of items. However, due to the urgency of time, some statistical systems have not yet been fully prepared, so they are not listed in detail here. Among them, there is one item worth more than several thousand yuan. This cannot be determined by the number of items. The total expenditure for library and instrument equipment, excluding those that have been determined but not yet paid, has reached 389,280 yuan. The total cost of buildings, library, and instrument equipment is 838,742 yuan.

5. Expanding the Area of ​​School Property In the past two academic years, the area of ​​school property has increased significantly. With the kindness of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, it was decided to allocate the Wulong and Mufu mountain forest farms in the suburbs to the school. The area of ​​Wulong Mountain is more than 7,700 mu, and the area of ​​Mufu Mountain is more than 6,000 mu, totaling more than 13,700 mu. Land was also purchased in Kunshan Jiangpu to expand the farm, totaling 118 mu. In addition, a sixth dormitory for faculty and staff was purchased near the main campus, costing 11,804 yuan (this was purchased at the end of the 21st year of the Republic of China, before the new campus site was determined). This is the general situation of increasing school property.

6. Centralizing the Location of Colleges for Observation and Convenience. In the past, the offices, teaching, and research locations of each college were very scattered. Some departments of the same college were located in different places, and even in one department, various courses were taught and experimented in different places. After several planning sessions, they are now more centralized. Zhongshan College is now the College of Liberal Arts, the Science Museum is the main building of the College of Science, Southeast College is the College of Law, Nanguo College is the main building of the College of Education, the new classroom is the main building of the College of Engineering, and the College of Agriculture has always been concentrated in Sanpailou, so there is no change.

Spring and Autumn Children's Weekly

How to Train Our Bodies

— Gong Jitang

A famous Westerner said: "A happy spirit resides in a strong body." What he meant was: "With a strong body, there is a happy spirit."

I think every child knows that a weak body is most susceptible to illness, and illness is very painful. So how can we make our bodies strong? Simply put:

1. Don't eat snacks, and don't eat too much at meals;

2. Do not eat irritating foods (such as cigarettes, tea, etc.)

3. Do not eat raw and unclean things;

4. Get up early and go to bed early, and have regular rest;

5. Pay attention to the weather and add or subtract our clothes;

6. Bathe often to keep your body clean.

I think children have already heard these points from the teachers in the school. The reason why I repeat them now is that I hope the children will keep them in mind and practice them every day, so that every child will have a lively and healthy body.

How Did Yan Hui Become a Great Sage?

— Jin Rong

Children! Do you know Yan Hui, a great sage of thousands of years ago? He was a student of Confucius. When he was young, his family was very poor. At that time, his classmates often bullied him and even said that he stole things. Later, when Confucius found out, he wanted to test Yan Hui's character.

One day, a piece of silver was found in Yan Hui's desk, with a note attached, which read "Heaven bestows Yan Hui a piece of silver." After reading it, he wrote "Unexpected wealth does not enrich a poor man" and put it back in place.

After this test, Confucius knew that Yan Hui was a good student, so he taught him all his talents, and he became a great sage.

Mutual Help

— Nai Chang

Early in the morning, leaning against the window and looking down at the street, I saw two pitiful people. Children, who do you think are the most pitiful people in the world? Aren't they those homeless, hungry, and cold beggars? But the two beggars I saw were the most pitiful among the pitiful; because one was legless and the other was blind!

A legless person cannot run, and a blind person cannot see the road. But these two pitiful people were smart. They combined the parts of each person that were not disabled and became a healthy person!

How did they combine? It's that the blind person carries the legless person on his back. The blind person has legs, and they are healthy legs; the legless person has eyes, and they are healthy eyes. In this way, when they combine, they become a person with bright eyes and healthy legs!

This scene touched me and made me think that people should help each other, shouldn't they, children? If we can all help each other, use our strengths to help others, and use the strengths of others to make up for our own shortcomings, we can all run on the bright road in big strides; in this way, we will not regress or decline!

Great Children

— Qin Yunxian

Children, children,

Great children.

We are all the masters of the country,

The entire destiny of the country in the future,

Is tied to our hands,

Our responsibility; is so heavy.

Now we must train our bodies,

Now we must study hard,

We have strong muscles and arms,

We have a mind full of knowledge,

In the future, we can win glory for the country.

Children, children,

Great children.

Soda

— Duxin

One afternoon, Dad opened a soda for Ming'er to drink. As soon as the bottle cap was opened, the gas followed the water from the bottle into the glass. So, Ming'er asked; "Dad, I have drunk soda, but I don't know what this gas is. Can you tell me today?"

"The gas that comes out? Let me tell you, it's carbonic acid gas," Dad said.

"Carbonic acid gas, Dad, I don't want to drink it anymore. The teacher said that this gas is harmful to our body," Ming'er shook his head and said.

"Ha! You're wrong, Ming'er. You only know that it's harmful to the lungs, but you don't know that it's beneficial to the stomach. Now, you're not inhaling this gas, but drinking this gas. Inhaling it, it goes to the lungs and is harmful, but drinking it, it goes to the stomach and is beneficial to you. Drink it quickly, child, Dad will have a glass too."

So, Ming'er smiled, and he quickly drank the soda. But Dad said again.

"Ming'er, I'm telling you, you can't drink too much soda. If you drink too much, your digestion will be in poor condition, because it contains alkaline baking soda. Everything in the world, eating less is always more delicious!"

The Origin of Shoes

— Jingying

Children, aren't you wearing shoes every day? But do you know its origin? Now I will tell you some!

People before the invention of shoes had no shoes to wear. All day long, they walked barefoot in the thorny mountains and forests, living a barbaric life. However, the king's palace was paved with brocade carpets. One day, when the king married the princess of a neighboring country, the king ordered that ten miles of carpets be laid from the front of the palace, and he stood on it to welcome his beautiful queen. After waiting for a long time, he still did not see her come. The king was very anxious, so he walked forward. When he walked to the end of the ten-mile-long carpet, he heard the sound of a group of horseshoes galloping from far to near. Then came a group of cavalry, with his beautiful queen in the middle. The king could not help but forget everything and ran to embrace her. Later, when he returned to the palace, he found that the soles of his feet were scratched by stones. He was very frustrated, but he could not think of a proper solution. Soon, his queen came up with this plan. She summoned the smartest people in the country, cut animal skins into shapes similar to the soles of the feet, and used ropes to tie them to the feet. So the king was very happy and ordered all the people of the country to make this foot protection item.

How Far Is the Earth from the Sun?

— Hua

From the Earth we stand on to the Sun we look at, the distance in between, according to astronomers, is 93 million miles, equivalent to 260 million Chinese miles. Exactly how far this number is, is still unclear in our minds; we can't imagine how far.

Now, let's use a few metaphors to illustrate, and everyone will be surprised when they hear it.

It Would Take Two and a Half Years to Count

If we spend one minute counting from one to two hundred, then we can count to 288,000 every day and night, without eating or sleeping, non-stop for twenty-four hours each day; this number is about one-323rd of 93 million. So, it would take 323 days, or ten and a half months, to finish counting this number. This is without stopping for even one second. If we calculate according to the current "three-eight system," we should add three times the time, which would be thirty-one months plus a few days, or two years plus a few days. Do you think this distance is far?

It Would Take 358 Years to Travel by Beijing-Shanghai Train

The Beijing-Shanghai express train travels at 30 miles per hour. If we travel from the Earth to the Sun at the speed of the Beijing-Shanghai train, it would take 358 years to reach it. Assuming we set off during the Wuchang Uprising, we wouldn't reach the Sun and see its wonders until 257 years of the Republic of China.

It Would Take 54 Years to Travel by Airplane

The fastest way to travel is by airplane. If we travel by a biplane flying at 197 miles per hour, it would only take three hours to fly from Beiping to Nanjing. But to fly from the Earth to the Sun, it would take 54 years. Children! If you are eleven years old this year and set off from the ground, flying towards the Sun, then by the time you stop on the Sun, you will be a sixty-five-year-old man with a white beard!

Shanghai Children's Happiness Committee held the first lecture in the Family Education Lecture Series, in which kindergarten students of Shanggong Elementary School performed "Striving to Resist the Enemy," four little treasures.

— Zhuojie

A Practitioner of the New Life Movement

— Ge Shoumin, a student of Shanghai Minsheng Elementary School

What is the New Life? The New Life just teaches us how to be human. To make the country strong, we must implement the New Life; to implement the New Life, we must first train ourselves.

Who do you think is a practitioner of the New Life Movement? Not a great man in politics, not a hero in the military, not an inventor with agile thoughts, but a young apprentice in a national goods store. He gets up early every day, works diligently, respects his teachers and elders, loves his colleagues, pays attention to cleanliness, and also works hard. He still reads for an hour in the morning before the store opens. It is a pity that he cannot go to bed early at night because of his low position and job. If he were born in a wealthy family, he could really make a career in the future.

This young apprentice has already practiced the New Life. Let's get up quickly and implement the New Life Movement.

The Frog's Transformation

— Dun

Gak gak gak, gak gak gak,

My belly is white, my back is green.

When I was young, I had a tail, but when I grew up, I was bald,

First I entered the water, then I landed on land,

I protect the rice fields and catch pests.

Gak gak gak, gak gak gak.

The Simplest Animated Shadow Play

— Mi Shutong

Materials: White paper, pencil, scissors. Production method: Cut two strips of white paper with scissors, one and a half inches wide and about five inches long, stack them together, and then use a pencil to draw a crying face on the left end of the top strip of paper, and a smiling face on the same end of the bottom strip of paper. Then, wrap the top strip of paper around the pencil to give it some elastic recoil. Now you can start playing. Playing method: Align the paper strips on the table, press down on the right end of the paper strips with your right hand, and move our pencil left and right along the paper strips. At that time, you will see a face that sometimes cries and sometimes smiles, as if it is going crazy.

Children, you can draw other things on the paper strips yourself, and you will have the same interest. This game is very simple, but there are a few things to pay attention to. First, the white paper must be slightly stiff, otherwise it will not have elastic recoil; second, the drawing should be clear, and the drawings on the upper and lower paper strips should match, otherwise it will not be clear.

Small Talk on Summer Hygiene

Food on Stalls

— Jianfen

Children, summer is here! On both sides of the road, you can see many stalls, with a wide variety of food on the stalls, such as water chestnuts, candied plums, peanut candy... countless varieties.

Speaking of the equipment of the stalls, there is only a wooden board and a pole that can be carried for walking; other than the food being sold, there is nothing else in the pole. The stall owners put the food being sold on the wooden board, letting the sand and ash accumulate on it, and the flies stop on it. As long as the food is sold, that's all; hygiene is not discussed at all.

Therefore: Children who like to buy snacks at stalls: when you buy them, first check the food to see if there is sand and ash accumulated on it! Are there any fly eggs on it! These are all things that should be paid attention to before buying and eating. If you find sand and ash and fly eggs on the food, then you might as well endure your cravings and not buy it to eat; because if you carelessly buy it and eat it, you will feel unwell in your stomach, or even get sick.

Finally: I hope the little friends who like to buy snacks at the stalls: quickly change this bad habit and don't go to unhygienic stalls to buy things to eat.

The Cat and the Fox

— Chengzhao

Once, a cat and a fox were sitting together in the forest, chatting.

The fox said, "No matter what important things happen, I don't care. Because I have all kinds of clever tricks that can solve all difficulties."

The fox also said, "Ms. Cat, what will you do if you are suddenly attacked or threatened by someone?"

The cat smiled and replied to the fox, "Mr. Fox, I only have one plan. If this plan doesn't work, then I can only die!"

The fox frowned and said, "Madam, I am very worried about you. I wanted to teach you a few clever tricks, but it is not appropriate to rely on others. We should still take care of ourselves."

The fox had just finished speaking when a large group of hunting dogs attacked them both with all their might.

With his only agility, the fox climbed up a tree and sat quietly on a branch.

Although the fox had many clever tricks, it could not escape, and was bitten to death by the hunting dogs.

Children, the safe plan is not about having many. You can know this by looking at the fox's death!

Rural Children's Correspondence

— Ziming

Dear Children:

Silkworm babies hatch from tiny black spots: they sleep a few times and shed their outer clothes several times; their black and yellow bodies become bright, crystal-clear, snow-white, and fat babies, climbing onto the silkworm mountain, spinning silk to make cocoons, and hiding inside. In a few days, they come out again, and at this time, they become silkworm moths with wings that cannot fly far, laying eggs on paper.

The rice seedlings in the paddy fields are all growing vigorously. Frogs use their hind legs to jump around: opening their big mouths, many small insects are always buried in their bellies. So they triumphantly play a triumphal song. Suddenly, with a "wa" sound, this triumphant fellow is caught and wrapped by a snake mother; a few minutes pass, and he becomes someone else's bread. Frog! Poor frog!

Because the snake mother is full, her swimming is also a bit sluggish; she is seen by a little friend, who shoulders a bamboo stick and hits the snake, hitting it right on the head and killing it. Snake, do you still remember the triumphant time when you ate the field frog?

Friends, frogs eat small insects, snakes eat frogs, and little friends hit snakes. Although these are small things in the animal kingdom; but, in the world, there is power and hegemony, bullying the weak. This is a microcosm for us to see, and we should carefully savor it!

Children All Over the World

— Xiao Jianqing

(1) This is a child from India. The place where they live is very hot. Most of them run naked in the sun or play by the sea. They also keep very long hair, wrapped in five-colored cloth.

(2) This is a child from the Philippines. His body is as black as chocolate. He doesn't wear clothes, and he often wears a piece of cloth on his lower body.

(3) This is an American native. Look how beautiful his clothes are. His skin is red. He likes hunting, archery, and decorating with crow feathers.

(4) These are children from Egypt. The place where they live is mostly desert and very hot, but they wear very large clothes and wrap their heads. Their shoes are very similar to Chinese shoes.

Women's World My Ideal Future Life Special Issue

Preface

— Editor

All human beings, as long as they are not idiots, have their future aspirations.

An ideal future not only requires individual efforts, but also has a close relationship with the era and society at that time. If we disregard the progress of the times and the changes in the social environment, and blindly fantasize, that is just a fool's dream.

China in this era, Chinese young women in this era. Living in this colonial environment, what exactly is their ideal future life like? This is worth paying close attention to. This is also the motive for publishing this special issue.

The result of soliciting articles was that the number of applicants was beyond our expectations. But the regret is that most of the hardworking and distressed women not only cannot express their expectations in this small garden, but they have not even acquired the ability to read! In addition, they are either busy with life or do not pay attention to the news, so they naturally miss the opportunity. Therefore, although we received many manuscripts, we can only say that they are a minority among the minority. However, in this minority, we can also see several types, such as (1) those who are infatuated with rosy dreams, (2) those who yearn for a single life, (3) those who hate the city and want to escape to the countryside, (4) those who only want to dedicate themselves to society, and (5) those who take the transformation of the entire society as a prerequisite.

China is still China, China is still a semi-colonial country, how many women can have a happy life? How many women can find a suitable job? Where is the happy land in the countryside? Where should we go? Smart people will understand, right?

(I)

— Pan Xuezhen

Suppose I am already married. My husband would naturally be very happy with me, because now he is already very intimate with me, and very understanding of me.

Under the shade of swaying green willows and blooming red peach blossoms, appears the residence of my husband and I. Quietly and serenely silent, only the sound of cicadas can be heard. There, I lean alone against the window, knitting his wool sweater. Suddenly I hear footsteps. It turns out he has returned. Oh! Before I knew it, it was already half past five.

Now I am no longer making wool sweaters. What I am sewing in my hands are children's clothes, because I am already six months pregnant.

After a long time, one evening, he embraces his child, kissing him. He says how lovely this little angel is. Indeed, since I had her, I have been extraordinarily happy.

This is a glimpse of my ideal future life.

(II)

— Pinxian

Lately, when I come into contact with the opposite sex, I can't help but feel shy. I am startled to realize that I am already a mature virgin (Village girls are raised in their mother-in-law's home and get married as early as ten years old!).

When I am alone, under the moon, among the flowers, even in my dreams, I anticipate the future, the future?

I will first carefully choose my eternal partner. Our union will be based on love, and cannot succumb to a commercial transaction.

My husband should be an intelligent, healthy young man who can make a living, regardless of his profession, and without any bad habits.

If possible, I will leave my parents-in-law and form a small family with my husband.

Our study will be filled with famous works of international translations, science, politics, and literature; if my husband is a businessman, there will also be some business news.

At home, I will prepare more nutritious and easily digestible dishes like vegetables and eggs. When my husband returns from the office, I will carefully prepare the dishes and bring them to his table. When my husband is busy eating, I think: he will appreciate the goodness of his wife.

But I would like to entrust the housework to a female servant and find a suitable job for myself.

We will of course have children. If I give birth to a girl in my first pregnancy, when someone asks, I don't want to hear my husband sigh and say, "Just a girl!" A good daughter is equal to a good son.

When we are free, my head rests in my husband's arms, the child's arms embrace my legs, and my husband hums love poems about pickled mustard greens or the Song of Everlasting Regret: "In the heavens, may we be birds flying wing to wing; on earth, may we be trees with branches twined from limb to limb!"

We all know how to love our country, care about national affairs, and love to use domestic goods.

Whether they are boys or girls, we will send our children to schools that are suitable for the needs of society. I will give them a sweet kiss every day, and they will repay me with filial piety.

Chastity must be mutually maintained by men and women. If my husband has an affair with a young girl, or if anyone else has one, I will immediately divorce him without hesitation.

Finally, there is no feast in the world that does not end. If I die before my husband, I promise my husband to remarry, and vice versa.

(III)

— Heng

Ah! It is shameful to say. The life of my dreams is envisioned in my mind almost every day, but dreams are always just dreams.

Like a ship without a rudder, I have spent my past dreamlike life in the tide of humanity, filled with suffering, sorrow... I have tried several times to reform my psychology, change my ideals to adapt to the environment, but I cannot, I will never be able to. I just hope, I always hope!

I hope that one day I can escape the infighting of my large family, and go with him to form a small family that can realize our ideals, and live our poetic life together!

Get up when the sky is just beginning to brighten, tidy up the housework, and then lead my two or three children to the park to enjoy the supreme enjoyment of nature: do some calisthenics myself, and then teach them to play ball, sail small boats, read books and newspapers... spend this first half of the day (of course, the older children must be sent to school, and lunch must be taken care of myself).

In the afternoon, I will take on half a day of schoolwork at a small school to increase some income and help with expenses.

At night, under his guidance, I will read some books to increase some necessary knowledge, and at the same time supervise the children

to review their homework from the day.

This is the future life of my dreams, perhaps shallow enough to be laughable!

(IV)

— Jingqi

I have grown up in the city since I was a child, but the future life of my dreams! I hope to be in the countryside, which contains poetry and conveys meaning to the fullest extent.

In front, there is a boundless wheat field, with a small stream and weeping willows on both sides, and lush green trees behind. Amidst this environment, there is a thatched cottage. Except for two windows and a door, it is covered with ivy. The walls inside are light yellow, and are decorated with sky blue palace lanterns. The furniture is a complete set of cream-colored, small, exquisite, Western-style furniture. In the middle hangs a portrait of a loving mother who loves with all her heart. On the table are the calligraphic and painting works of the loving mother. I will be the owner of this house, with an old woman and two beautiful kittens. I get up at dawn and take a walk in the fields and water flowers. Then I have breakfast and write large and small characters, and practice cursive script. After lunch, I rest until dinner, and I am writing manuscripts all the time. I make a living by selling articles. In the meantime, if I feel tired, I will play the pipa and blow the xiao. After dinner, I will go with the old woman to listen to stories and myths from the neighboring farmers. I will go to the city once a month to visit my parents, see relatives and friends, and collect manuscript fees, and I hope to often encounter some unexpected little things to regulate the ordinary and boring life.

In addition, there will be a noble and talented friend of the opposite sex, who will be my lifelong confidant, but I will never marry him, and I will not meet him often, but I will often communicate with him and conduct various academic discussions, which will be considered spiritual comfort only. Besides this, I will never associate with a third person of the opposite sex, and even my friends of the same sex will be no more than three or five people at most.

Well, if my future life can be like this, then my ideal will be realized.

(V)

— Zhao Junyu

I am a seventeen-year-old girl; a student studying at a midwifery school. I don't hope to be a great person in the political world in the future, a famous person in society, or to enjoy some noble life; but I also have a goal to move forward, and this goal can represent what my ideal future life is. Of course, this ideal may seem too small to women with great ambitions.

What is this goal? It is to hope to become a successful obstetrician who can maintain the health and safety of mothers and babies in the future.

In China, where science is underdeveloped, everything lags behind others. Even obstetrics, which uses scientific methods to deliver babies, has only attracted the attention of Chinese people in recent years, and people have only begun to advocate it and learn it. However, short-term efforts cannot overthrow the old forces in one fell swoop: the old methods of delivery are still deeply rooted and difficult to defeat. Those old women (i.e., midwives) who have no knowledge and completely rely on fate still fill the society and occupy a large position. Therefore, one can often see in newspapers many records about old women who have injured mothers by mistake, and one can also hear similar unfortunate narrations from people's mouths. I have personally seen a relative die at the hands of an ignorant old woman during childbirth. This terrible phenomenon makes me feel that it is really necessary for us women to work hard to study obstetrics and eliminate the old-fashioned midwives. Because the death of one person is of course a loss to the country, and the weakness of a mother and baby has a great impact on the health of the nation! Therefore, after graduating from junior high school, I transferred to a midwifery school to study. I will graduate next year. After graduation, I decided to first practice in an obstetrics hospital for a few years, using the existing knowledge in books as the basis for on-the-spot practical exploration. At that time, I thought that no matter what, I would not muddle-headedly kill the mother.

In these few years, I am working hard to build the foundation for realizing my ideal life. After I have considerable ability, I will unite with a few others to open an obstetrics hospital in the inland, and at the same time, using methods that gradually win people's hearts, promote the benefits of scientific delivery and the dangers of old-fashioned delivery, so as to invisibly defeat the power of the old women. Then, depending on my ability, I will establish one or several midwifery schools to train midwifery talents and replace the old women's positions. Although the old forces are very difficult to eradicate, if everyone can do their best, then there is nothing in the world that cannot be done!

This is the future life of my dreams, this life

is of course extremely hard and has no great hope, but I believe that being able to become an obstetrician who is beneficial to the health of the nation is not meaningless.

(VI)

— Chen Xiuling

"Ideals are beautiful, facts are sad." Of course, I am no exception. The ideal future life cannot escape the beautiful ideal.

The future life of my dreams is to hope to be a teacher, getting along with that group of lively, lovely, innocent children every day.

Because children are the masters of the future country, they are urgently in need of good education and cultivation.

Although my academic ability is not high and I have no experience to speak of, because I am still studying in the second year of high school normal school, I will not spare any effort to do it, because this is my interest and aspiration, especially my responsibility.

As a teacher, I can make efforts to study the knowledge I want to study in the spare time in the evening and morning, and I must also study a good, new education system to replace the current education system that I am not satisfied with.

On Saturday afternoons and Sundays, I will take a walk in the park, or invite colleagues to play in the suburbs. In this way, the fatigue of a week's work can be easily sent away here. If there is still spare time, I can read books, or invite a few children who are usually more clever to play the piano and sing songs together to regulate this educational life.

The life of a teacher is the most beautiful life. The future life of my dreams is to live this beautiful life of a teacher.

(VII)

— Xuan

It is probably mostly due to the influence of my parents that I have unconsciously developed this tendency to be indifferent to fame and fortune and almost want to live in seclusion. I have never admired any extravagance since I was a child, and this tendency seems to be more obvious as I grow up. I have also lived in the city for quite some time. The civilization of the city cannot tempt me, a person from the mountains and fields. The tense air in the city makes people breathe, and the skin, flesh, and bones of the whole body will also become tense and uncomfortable. After this powerful test, I am even more convinced that I am not worthy of living in this atmosphere. I hate that kind of life, I despise that so-called urban civilization, what I need is a simple, tranquil, and leisurely life. At this time when the country is so chaotic, this requirement may be scolded, but this is, after all, a requirement, or a dream. Whether it can be realized is still unknown. Even if it can be realized, it will have to be many years later. When I am old, if I encounter this kind of tranquil life again, perhaps it can still be forgiven.

My hometown is a small semi-rural town. Although it has not lost its original rural atmosphere, it has been dyed with many urban habits, so I still have more dislike for it. In the future, if possible, I want to live in a very simple village with mountains and rivers. The houses are sufficient for living and use, there is a wide square for exercise, and there is land around to grow things. I will live with companions who have similar hobbies and interests. It is best to have one who is older and one who is younger. The older one has experience and judgment, because I have too little experience, especially little judgment. Therefore, I definitely need such a person. Younger people are more energetic and can accompany me in activities so that I will not get old. I think that the increase in a person's age is not the easiest thing to make a person old, only the lack of vigor is dangerous. I am afraid of seeing those people who are old and decadent before they are old.

Every day, in addition to necessary work, there is a fixed time for reading, time for singing, playing musical instruments, and spare time for exercise. The open space next to the house is for us to grow our own things. I like this kind of farming the most. The harvested things are for our food and clothing. Or there is a risk of not having enough, so we must first gather some property as a fund, and start accumulating before this ideal is realized.

This is an ideal without any extravagance. Perhaps it can be fulfilled, but if there are no companions and no funds, then the ideal will always be an ideal, and my body will only be able to float and sink in the crowd.

(VIII)

— Fangping

I have grown up in the countryside since I was a child. In the countryside, the humble status of women is shocking to say. My mother and I, under the shackles of thousands of years of traditional feudalism, have tasted a lot of miserable and inhuman life; until now, due to the invasion and oppression of international imperialists, the countryside is increasingly in bankruptcy, and our general women are living like pigs and dogs under the pressure of life. When men get angry and come home, we can be said to be the only objects of their anger. It is as if all their poverty is caused by us.

In real life, experience tells me: if we are not to be bound by the old feudal forces and old ethics, we must not depend on men economically, and our economy must be on an equal footing with men; and the liberation of women in general is not a partial problem, but a social problem as a whole. If the social system does not seek a fundamental solution, the so-called women's problem will also be impossible to solve, because first of all, we cannot get rid of economic dependence, get rid of being a man's private property, or even a commodity; first of all, we cannot allow the majority of women to get rid of poverty and enjoy a true human life.

Therefore, the ideal life I envision for the future is not the kind of happy and ideal family that the average lady dreams of, because this has become impossible for us. In reality, life does not allow us to have such a good dream, and what we hope for is that the majority of our women have a true human life, and I hope to seek a solution to this from the overall social problem!

Therefore, the future life of my dreams is that I want to start from now, try my best to overcome my old nature, strengthen my consciousness, and recognize the mission I bear in women: in the practice of life, I will, together with women who are under the same multiple pressures of life, seek the way to truly liberate women in the future life.

In the future life, I hope not to have a slave-like marriage, to submerge the meaning of my life as a "person," but I may as well get married if it does not harm my work and if there is a suitable opportunity. As for a happy family, I only hope for it when everyone is happy.

As long as I am advancing on the road of "being a person," as long as I can do enough of what I can in the process of women's liberation, so that we will eventually have a day to be a person, this is the future life of my dreams.

(IX)

— Fengzi

The reason why human beings can still struggle to live in extreme pain is because they have an ideal for the future of life, which can make them forget the past, endure the present, and hope for the future. However, because the environment is different, everyone has their own ideals, and there is an ideal for every era. I remember when I was studying at a normal school in the twelfth or thirteenth year of the Republic of China, because I read Ms. Bingxin's works such as The Lost, Superman, etc., and Tagore's Stray Birds, plus a kind of writing that was very popular at that time, I was influenced by that kind of writing, and my dream was full of truth, goodness, beauty, and love. In fact, my life was very poor and painful at that time, but because my heart was beautified for a while, I ignored the pain I was suffering at the moment. Since graduating in the fifteenth year of the Republic of China until now, what I have experienced and felt in these eight years has made me realize that my dream was wrong; I understand that there is no truth, goodness, beauty, and love in the current society, but it is used to decorate this dark society. I don't want to do this kind of self-deceiving dream anymore. Now I want to understand that we are in an extremely tense life, the economic aggression of imperialism is intensifying day by day, a group of men are oppressed by the economy to the point where they cannot breathe, and we women are living a life of slaves under slaves under multiple oppressions, what leisure do we have to do that leisurely and elegant dream? But I am not completely desperate. My ideals are:

1. To have something to do in society and be economically independent.

2. Men and women should be combined based on the same interests and harmonious feelings, without any restrictions, and no one should dominate anyone.

3. There should be good nurseries and public kitchen facilities in the society, so that we can get rid of this family burden and concentrate on doing our own business.

4. During pregnancy and childbirth, we can have adequate rest, and our career and salary will not be affected. In this way, women can be free people.

I know that although my ideals are not very high, it is very difficult to realize them, because the life of an individual is a corner of the entire society. Only with a rational society can we talk about

the day when my ideal life will be realized.

(X)

— Liaoer

On September 18th, the iron hooves of Japan stepped into my hometown of Shenyang. At that time, I was in the dormitory of a certain university in the old capital, having a sweet dream! When I woke up, I couldn't go home anymore. Pain, panic, resentment, and annoyance filled my heart. I saw that some of my classmates were stomping their feet and beating their chests, wanting to join the army, and some were leisurely and carefree without caring about anything. There were even... I don't want to write about it anymore here. The past is gone. Now that I am living in Shanghai, which is half foreign, I have other reveries:

"1934" has been half-rolled away by the wheel of time, and "1936" is not just around the corner? Death rays, poison gas, germ bombs, and poison needle cannons are already openly and secretly being invented and manufactured? We are certainly all clamoring about how to save the country, but in such a chaotic situation, how can we, these disorganized and untrained lumps of flesh, meet this future disaster? When that disaster comes, perhaps there is no way to hide or avoid it. We, who have no weapons in our hands, naturally have to fight with our flesh! But we also need to be organized.

I look forward to the bright clouds in the future. But we must unite to cross this death line. This is the life I hope to realize in the nearest future.

(XI)

— Zigang

Like fish in the Yellow River, if the Yellow River floods, then all the fish, big and small, and even the fish eggs that are still being nurtured, will suffer the same fate, at most with different degrees of severity. This depends on whether the fish are at the focus or the tail end of the flood.

People cannot live without the environment they live in and the people of the same era. It may not be easy to be a hermit in the 20th century, and it seems that there are very few fools who claim to be aloof. When people are struggling for the truth, they will not hesitate at all and will move forward bravely in a solid group.

If people are not blind or deaf, they will more or less feel a little frightened by the chaotic affairs of this world standing on the dividing line. Those who are near the muzzles and blades will undoubtedly scream in the shooting, followed by those who are a little farther away braving the bullets and blades to rescue, which is also self-help at the same time. People always care about things that are related to their own part of the position, unless they are blinded by psychedelic drugs, they will not be indifferent.

At the junction of darkness and light, on the eve of the struggle between truth and demons, the drastic upheaval is inevitable and unavoidable. People may complain about being unfortunate to be born in this upheaval, but can't it be said to be a kind of happiness? This is a tight and stimulating life!

Therefore, in this great decision, we must prepare ourselves and not be onlookers. Of course, in fact, we are definitely not allowed to.

Women seem to be like blind people covered with double cloths, but when humanity wakes up, our cloths will be removed, the light will reappear in front of us, and we can run on the right and wrong paths, whichever we want.

The facts also tell us to run to the side of the public reason of the majority of people, where is our powerful camp, which will give us encouragement and courage to fight for the stolen loot and fight for the fairness snatched with blood and flesh.

We don't covet the peace and happiness of seeking temporary comfort. This world will not allow you to be at ease, hesitate, or doze off, otherwise you will be trampled into cannon fodder.

At the end of the cliff, on the bank of the river where the bridge is broken, resolutely decide your own path, people will sacrifice the small self and move forward on the position of the big self. The light of the future is anxiously burning people's hearts.

There are no heroes, only countless soldiers marching in the same big team, based on the public belief.

Countless privates, I am also one of them.

Finance Under Sustained Selling Pressure, Bullion Price Breaks Through the 1,000 Yuan Barrier, | Continuing to Fall by 7.9 Jiao |

Since the sudden price drop in the gold market the day before yesterday, public sentiment has been pessimistic, and it is difficult to see a resurgence. Therefore, this morning, the overseas silver market exchange rates did not increase much. However, public sentiment was already weary, making it difficult to pull prices up. As a result, the 1,000 yuan barrier was finally breached, and a selling atmosphere permeated the market. Fortunately, it was almost noon, and the Central Bank intervened with spot purchases and Guangbang's acceptance of delivery notes, slightly curbing the selling trend. At the beginning of the morning, the overseas silver market saw the British pound rise and the US dollar remain stable. The difference between near-term and far-term silver prices on the Gold and Silver Exchange was negligible, with near-term prices slightly lower and far-term prices slightly higher. Exchange rates opened higher but closed lower. London spot gold rose by half a penny, US cotton fell by nine points, US wheat rose by six and a quarter points, and stocks fell by 1.57 yuan. The various telegrams from the day before yesterday have already been detailed in the newspapers. Raw material prices opened higher at eight yuan, but ultimately trended downward due to oversupply and downstream weakness. By the time pre-market trading opened, the situation was extremely weak. After the opening, bank demand was healthy, and although it was relatively stable, news of HSBC's exchange rate quotes showing the British pound up 1.25 and the US dollar up 0.25 led to strong selling pressure from suppliers, and the situation became one of sideways trading, contending around five yuan. When the Seattle overnight silver price report came in, showing a rise of 1.25 and no change, the short sellers took advantage of the situation to amplify their efforts, and the selling trend began to take shape. This was because public sentiment was already uneasy, and the bulls were more restrained. Fellow traders aggressively filled the market with US dollar sales, and when the domestic market loosened, the downward momentum took hold. Unfavorable news, such as the US Treasury Department's gradual increase in silver purchases, which would inevitably lead to the issuance of more silver certificates, although unconfirmed, certainly contributed to the selling trend in the current declining market. The gold price gradually fell, and although there were large buyers intervening, they could not hold the price up. Bank demand was overwhelmed by the aggressive sales of fellow traders, and the domestic market suddenly became loose and flooded, leading to the breaking of the 1,000 yuan barrier. The Central Bank intervened with spot purchases, and Guangbang took the opportunity to buy at low prices, slightly raising the price. However, the 1,000 yuan level could not be sustained. As it approached the noon closing, banks took advantage of the low prices to cover their positions, and there were no major changes afterward. The price of pure gold was 1,014.7 yuan. The market conditions for the first half of the day are recorded below.

The morning opening was 1,005.7 yuan, down one yuan from the previous closing. Raw material prices opened at 5.6 yuan. Exchange rates opened with near-term selling prices of 1 shilling 3 pence 8125 for the British pound and 33.1875 yuan for the US dollar. Dadecheng, Hengyu, and Yuanchun all sold, retreating to 4.7 yuan. Pangeng bought August US dollars at 4375. Anticipating HSBC's exchange rate quotes showing the British pound up 1.25 and the US dollar up 0.25, Yuanmao, Yongsenchang, Yongda, Xingyongyi, Fengyongdadecheng, Hengyu, and others all sold, falling to 4.2 yuan. MacGalli covered October US dollars at 625, September at 5625, and remained stable. Tongfeng, Hengfu, Xingyongdadecheng, Daxingyonglai, and others entered, gradually rising to above 5 yuan. Mitsui Sumitomo covered October US dollars at 5625, and Huixiang worked hard to buy delivery notes, rising again to 5.8 yuan. Fuyu, Yuanmao, and Yong sold to within 5 yuan. At this time, Futaiheng and Fuan still accepted, pulling the price up by one yuan. However, because Shenkang and Fuyu still supplied, the situation was difficult to improve significantly. Tongyiyuanyi sold slightly, retreating to within 5 yuan. Yuanyida and Xingyong entered, but as public sentiment was downward, sellers in the market were brave. Senchangyong and Huixiang also sold, still falling to within 999 yuan. Banks covered October US dollars at 875 and stabilized. Hovering around the 9 yuan mark. The noon closing was 998.8 yuan. With Aggressive Selling by Chinese Merchants, Both British and US Exchange Rates Tend to Harden

▲HSBC Quotes the British Pound Up 1.25 and the US Dollar Up 0.25

According to foreign dispatches yesterday, London near-term and far-term both rose by 1.25, the US bank remained unchanged, near-term silver prices declined and far-term rose, London spot gold rose by half a penny, the British pound to the US dollar was 1.375, the US dollar to the British pound contracted by 0.375, the British pound to the French franc fell by 6 points, the US dollar to the French franc was unchanged, private dispatches reported silver prices as unchanged and stagnant, exchange rates fell by 0.25 and leveled off. The exchange market opened with near-term selling prices of 1 shilling 3 pence 8125 for the British pound and 33.1875 yuan for the US dollar, level for the British pound and tightening by 0.125 for the US dollar compared to the previous close. The market immediately loosened, but all banks were covering, and it seemed mediocre. Upon learning of HSBC's exchange rate quotes showing the British pound up 1.25 and the US dollar up 0.25, Chinese merchants were even more eager to sell. With the news of the Seattle overnight silver price rise of 1.25, bank demand turned sluggish, and unfavorable rumors spread. Chinese merchants and silver companies repeatedly sold off, and the exchange rates hardened further. The Central Bank intervened with spot intervention, and there were still buyers taking advantage of the low prices. The noon close showed near-term selling prices of 1 shilling 3 pence 9375 for the British pound and 33.5 or 33.5625 yuan for the US dollar, loosening by 0.125 for the British pound and hardening by 0.25 for the US dollar compared to the previous close. Chinese merchants collectively sold approximately 700,000 US dollars. Silver companies also flooded the market with sales. Bank demand was healthy, and they also covered shillings. The transactions for the first half of the day are recorded below.

The British exchange opened with a near-term selling price of 1 shilling 3 pence 8125. Weekend Foreign Interbank Lending Rates Remain Unchanged

Yesterday, the foreign interbank lending rates remained largely unchanged, with both the morning and afternoon rates at 6%. The addition of water to the forward rate was only 2-3%, and ultimately it was a white draw, with a plain and unremarkable situation. Moreover, yesterday was Saturday, and because of the afternoon holiday, the banks' settlement procedures were unusually simple. Interbank bill transactions in the market were over 3.4 million in the morning, and new transactions and afternoon transactions were each over 200,000. Transactions in the Small General Association were over 300,000. Foreign collateral loan transactions involved redeeming over 600,000 and making new loans of over 1.1 million. Banknotes withdrawn amounted to over 600,000 and issued amounted to over 900,000. Customer sources were 200,000 and outflows were 300,000. Bank settlements involved foreign banks settling over 1.3 million in bill payments and over 2.9 million in various telegraphic transfers, collateral, and miscellaneous payments. Settlement of accounts involved over 1.2 million, and withdrawals from warehouses amounted to 200,000. Chinese banks settled over 2 million in bill payments and over 3.8-3.9 million in various goods, foreign exchange, tax collateral, and miscellaneous payments. Settlement of accounts involved over 2 million, and withdrawals from warehouses amounted to 200,000. The market situation leveled off before closing, and some stocks recovered slightly. The small exchange also fell, and bonds were mixed and slightly lower. US Treasury bonds were particularly firm, and foreign bonds had no trend. French 7% bonds rose by more than one yuan, and other gains and losses were minimal. Grains also saw mixed gains and losses. Grains: Rumors of Korean Purchases of Wheat in Shanghai Drive Up Flour and Wheat Prices

Yesterday, the flour market opened in the morning, and all months showed a consistently strong trend. As the prices of foreign wheat in Chicago and Canada rebounded by about one to two jiao, market sentiment was naturally positive after the opening. Furthermore, the market had not wavered despite a significant decline in foreign wheat prices two days ago, which strengthened the confidence of both internal and external buyers. The limited offerings from major factories led many to speculate about potentially unfavorable actions by short sellers, thus increasing buying interest and driving prices higher. When the market opened in the afternoon, all months remained bullish, partly due to absorption by large long positions and partly due to the prolonged lack of rain. Longs spread rumors of Korean purchases of several hundred bags of wheat, further bolstering their position and increasing buying pressure. It is indeed unimaginable that the market would be so heavily influenced by outsiders after years of good harvests. As a result, the current month rose by two fen, July and August rose by two fen and seven li half, September rose by three fen, October rose by two fen and seven li half, and November rose by two fen.

After the opening of the wheat market in the morning, the prices for each month were generally stable. As the price of foreign wheat rebounded by only one to two jiao in Chicago and Canada, people did not pay much attention after the opening, and the prices for each month did not fluctuate much. However, when the market opened in the afternoon, there was a sudden and severe surge due to the rising flour market and widespread rumors that Korea was buying wheat in Shanghai. However, upon investigation, the quantity was only three to four hundred bags. In terms of location, it would be much more convenient to purchase in the north if there was a need. The industry insiders generally believe that the activity in Shanghai is a result of manipulation by the long positions. However, with this rumor, the market was greatly disturbed. From the opening to the closing, the price rose steadily. While the country is experiencing a good harvest, the only thing lacking is temporary rain, and people are unnecessarily disturbing themselves. If this situation continues, it may open a door for foreign wheat again. As a result, July rose by six fen, August rose by nine fen, September rose by eight fen, October rose by six fen, and November rose by nine fen. The spot wheat market was generally average. Special high-quality goods were slightly better by two or three fen. Guan Xuzhou wheat was priced at 2.99 yuan, Bengbu Mingguang wheat at 2.95 yuan, Liuhe Wuyi wheat at 2.85 yuan, Daqiao Yangzhou wheat at 2.82-3 yuan, Zhitang Penglai wheat at 2.78 yuan, Wuhu wheat at 2.76-7 yuan, Pukou wheat at 2.77 yuan, secondary at 2.75 yuan, Taizhou wheat at 2.84 yuan, Anqing wheat at 2.76 yuan, secondary at 2.73 yuan. Fuxin purchased 5,000 bags, Fufeng purchased 5,000 bags, and Xinda and Huafeng each purchased 2,000 bags.

Customer Xian Rice Sells Well, Price is High

▲ Strong Stomach for Domestic and Fuzhou Shipments

Yesterday, the customer Xian rice market was initially stable. However, because the Fuzhou gang was still greedy for stomach, and new domestic gangs and Zhejiang Wenzhou and Taizhou gangs arrived in the market, the market immediately saw an upward trend. The domestic gangs' appetite for stomach was no less than that of Fuzhou, and the local street also actively participated in purchases, so the market immediately showed an upward trend. Domestic gangs had not had a strong stomach for a long time. Now, due to the prolonged drought, farmland cannot be planted, and domestic rice prices and sentiment are trending upwards, so they are eager to purchase in Shanghai. Trading customers also took the opportunity to buy. Because the supply of goods is currently light, the market is rising accordingly. However, the market inventory is still sufficient. The activity of domestic gangs is temporary in nature, unlike the long-term nature of the Fuzhou gang. The current rice inventory is sufficient to meet the needs, and the market price is not easy to rise significantly. Only the high-quality rice in the market is not much, so various high-quality brown rice and machine-milled Xian rice have risen by five fen to nearly a jiao.
